							<div class="blog-stream blog-regular">
														<article id="post-16069" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-16069 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-culture category-dating category-faith category-relationships category-women">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-to-attract-a-woman-as-a-christian-man">How To Attract A Woman As A Christian Man</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/culture" rel="category tag">Culture</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/dating" rel="category tag">Dating</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/relationships" rel="category tag">Relationships</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/women" rel="category tag">Women</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-to-attract-a-woman-as-a-christian-man" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-11-07T10:00:11-05:00">
						November 7, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-11-03T18:01:43-04:00">
						November 3, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-to-attract-a-woman-as-a-christian-man#comments">40 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-to-attract-a-woman-as-a-christian-man">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-gym-bench-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>Young single women in the Orthodox Church don&#8217;t stay single for long. Since the ratio of young men to women is so high, it doesn&#8217;t take long for single women to be taken off the market. As Orthodox men calculate their prospects, a common question is asked: &#8220;How can I attract a woman?&#8221;</p>
<p>In the past, I developed a lifestyle around answering this question. It inevitably involved transforming myself into a man I thought women would be attracted to. I exaggerated my strengths, concealed my weaknesses, lied without ceasing, uprooted myself to locations where it was easier to meet women, and engaged in numerous sins to win over a woman&#8217;s fleeting affections. I can&#8217;t help but chafe when a man asks me how to attract a woman because&#8212;without spiritual considerations&#8212;the answer that &#8220;works&#8221; is to deceive and manipulate.</p>
<p>To attract a woman, one can mimic the approach of the Protestant Churches and be &#8220;seeker sensitive.&#8221; You could identify your target (the woman), find out her desires, and then mold yourself to satisfy them, even if that&#8217;s not who you are. You become a phony to, at the minimum, lie by omission so that she becomes attracted to the &#8220;best version of yourself.&#8221; You toss overboard the useful but socially mundane gifts that God has given you and instead summon qualities you don&#8217;t possess so that the women of this evil age lust after you. If they like a muscular man and you are puny, you hit the gym with urgent zeal. If they like a funny man and you are not, you practice comedy. If they like a &#8220;bad boy&#8221; but you are not, you must insinuate that you are a great sinner (if you served time in jail, that would be a plus in their eyes!). The whole idea of wanting to attract a woman presupposes that your current state is not attractive, and that you must transform both your physique and personality into that which pleases a woman to satisfy her in a carnal manner while using the flimsy pretext that it is all being doing for &#8220;spiritual&#8221; reasons.</p>
<p>Can you not already see how seeking to attract women makes an idol out of them? We are supposed to transform ourselves into children of God through prayer, obedience, and worship, and we attempt that with hardly any vigor, but when it comes to being liked by a woman, we are ready to change ourselves wholesale to be with a female creature who was made in <em>our</em> image. Indeed, wanting to attract a woman <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/men-treat-women-as-gods">inverts the natural order</a>, because we were made in the image of God and women <a href="https://www.biblegateway.com/passage/?search=Genesis+2%3A21-22&amp;version=NKJV">were made in the image of man</a>. Before you even meet her, by possessing a desire to win her over, you&#8217;ve already stepped foot into the pit. Without even knowing it, and in the most subtle of ways, she will control you as long as the ensuing relationship lasts, directly or indirectly.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16074" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/date-kiss-male-woman.jpg 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>Attempting to attract a woman through techniques or tactics is secular behavior, and I know this because I did it <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/8-personal-defects-that-allowed-me-to-worship-fornication-for-18-years">for nearly two decades</a>, and learned exclusively how to do so from secular sources. There is nothing Christian about modifying your essence and nature to be more pleasing to women than God while they are busy modifying their essence and nature to be more pleasing to men than God. There is nothing Christian about becoming handsome or socially astute through effort in order to excite a woman, to be vainglorious to attract the vainglorious. No, you do those things not to please God but to please yourself through the female flesh. I wholeheartedly condemn all efforts at &#8220;self-improvement&#8221; or &#8220;transformation&#8221; where the aim of your effort is to attract a woman instead of serve God. Men who are desperate to find a wife think they must attract a woman to please God when really they must please God so that He sends them a suitable woman. Surely it is better to evaluate a woman that God sends you versus one you met using sales tactics while talking to dozens of women on internet apps so that maybe one desires the result of your false transformation enough to get into a relationship with you.</p>
<p>The correct question to ask is this: How can I <em>identify</em> a woman who recognizes my love for Lord Jesus Christ? Instead of manually attracting a woman through superficial changes that clash with your God-given qualities and gifts, you instead use your eyes and ears to identify the one woman who wants you to lead her with faith. Notice the word &#8220;one.&#8221; You don&#8217;t need to attract a lot of women: you only need to find one woman who sees your own attraction for Christ. This means you can come across thousands of women who discard you as if you were trash, who do not see your love for God and call you all sorts of insulting names, and you will be tempted to fall into despair to think that no woman will ever love you, and be tempted to inject yourself with testosterone and wear cool skinny jeans like they do in Sweden, but you should deny that instinct, stay true to the faith, and wait for God to enlighten a woman that you are her match, and to enlighten you that she is your match, because <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/secular-marriage-vs-christian-marriage">an Orthodox marriage</a> is not a sales drive or a numbers game, but a game of patience and faith where we put our full trust in God to deliver what we need for our salvation and the salvation of others.</p>
<p>It is infinitely better for you to do a prostration to please God than a rep <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/4-reasons-why-lifting-in-gyms-is-a-bad-idea">at the bench press</a> to please a woman. It is better to make a spontaneous prayer glorifying God when you behold a beautiful mountain or vista than to make a worldly joke that you hope will make a woman laugh. It is better to shed tears of repentance at your sins than to puff out your chest to make a woman think you are an alpha male. I did all the latter and have nothing to show for it but darkness and sin. If you don&#8217;t think that you can get married using God alone, without tips and advice from the secular world of which I once preached, then you have not a woman problem but a <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/gods-revelation-to-the-human-heart">spiritual problem</a>.</p>
<p>Allow me to predict your future if you go on trying to attract a woman outside of the clean waters of the Church. In order to transform yourself into an &#8220;attractive&#8221; man, you will create a fantasy persona and wade into the sewage of the world, of dating apps and the like, and get the attention of a lukewarm woman who likes your personality, your skin-deep transformation, who transformed herself to attract a man and uses no less deception than you. You may enter a relationship with her, a pseudo-courtship infused with secular behaviors, because she was on the app after all and demands physical and emotional pleasure like all other women on the app, but you will rationalize to yourself that you&#8217;re doing God&#8217;s will and all will be fine. After some time passes, you become tired of wearing the mask, of being someone you&#8217;re not, but she is attracted to the mask, the false persona, the man full of self-pride and self-will, and you are scared to take it off because the pleasure and validation her affections give you will be withdrawn. Soon her secular flaws become more glaring as your attempt to flirt-to-convert her into the Church reveals that she&#8217;s only converting because she wants to receive the secular benefits of being a married woman, not because she wants to worship God in his True Church. You&#8217;re overly committed and don&#8217;t want to lose her. You fall for the false despairing notion that no other woman will love you due to your impatience and lack of trust in God. You decide to marry her before she flees into the arms of another man. How many good years will you have until the expensive bill comes due? I&#8217;ve seen this bill with my own eyes concerning other men, and let me tell you, this is a bill that is so expensive that no man can pay it in full. The payment plan lasts for the rest of your life, and if that&#8217;s God&#8217;s will for you then so be it, but I fail to see how using deception to hunt for secular women who were never serious about the faith in the first place is what God ordains for Orthodox men.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16075" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-1024x694.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="481" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-1024x694.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-300x203.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-768x520.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-1536x1041.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-1060x718.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-550x373.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-738x500.jpg 738w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-1594x1080.jpg 1594w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant-600x407.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/11/male-woman-distant.jpg 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>My advice for men essentially boils down to &#8220;be yourself,&#8221; but with a huge caveat: you are like Christ. Be yourself where yourself is Christ, who the Church <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-to-live-a-holy-life">teaches us to be like</a>, and identify a woman who wants to cleave into one flesh with an icon of Christ, of which you will be upon marriage as you establish a &#8220;little church&#8221; in your family home. What additional advice do you need in this case? You need to be a man with basic strength, courage, and communication ability. You need to notice when a woman stares at you for more than two seconds or when she asks around about you, and petition God to help you meet this woman and get to know her and discern if she could be your wife. That&#8217;s it! If you think I&#8217;m exaggerating, this is all I&#8217;m using in my own life, for anything else will kindle my passions and undoubtedly lead to sin. While I have reams of secular experience with women, and can analyze their behavior on the most minute level, it&#8217;s only useful when giving advice to other men in various stages of relationship difficulty, usually with women enflamed with worldly desires. For myself, however, I use my senses to identify which woman is interested in me and then my brain to discern her level of faith and then my heart to lean on God for help, because no matter how much experience you have with women, you will never see inside her soul and know for sure if she&#8217;s the one. It is effortless for her to pretend to be someone she&#8217;s not, whether subconsciously or otherwise, and since women are more socially advanced than men, you will be tricked and end up marrying a stranger, but know that God can see into her soul, and He knows who she really is, so don&#8217;t listen to me or other men when evaluating a particular woman: lean on God instead.</p>
<p>If you make googly eyes with a pretty woman and think to yourself how you can attract her, you&#8217;ve already lost. You&#8217;ve made her a false idol and have decided to trust your eyes and fallen flesh more than God. I pity you because you remind me of myself! You&#8217;re already in the pit and don&#8217;t know it. Through your weak faith and self-trust, you are about to make this woman into your god, and your inevitable fall may shatter you. I wish I can relay to you all the horror stories I&#8217;ve seen and heard that sum up thusly: the more desperate a man is to cleave to a secular woman, the more painful the outcome will be. It&#8217;s possible you may get an adorable child or two from it, but there will never be peace for them if the home is broken, and there is a high chance they will grow up to be broken themselves, and every day will be full of regret. Wake up, Christian man! A woman is not your God! Do not attempt to attract anything besides the grace of God within <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-to-join-the-orthodox-church">His Orthodox Church</a>, because you will be surely chastised, as I have been chastised, of wasting most of your life with secular women who keep your eyes away from God and onto the pleasures of your body and the feeding of your will and pride. Love God and simply wait for a woman who sees your love and wants to love God the way you do, and then you&#8217;ll have a good chance, and God will be with you. Whatever cross we have to bear in this life, whether it be a painful marriage, divorce, singledom, or something else we can&#8217;t foresee, may God give us the strength to bear it so that we retain our Orthodox faith until the end.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/33-things-christian-men-should-know-about-women"><em><strong>33 Things Christian Men Should Know About Women</strong></em></a></p>
										</div> <!-- .entry-content -->
																			</article>
																	<article id="post-16056" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-16056 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-faith category-orthodoxy">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/5-types-of-imagination-that-take-you-away-from-reality">5 Types Of Imagination That Take You Away From Reality</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/orthodoxy" rel="category tag">Orthodoxy</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/5-types-of-imagination-that-take-you-away-from-reality" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-10-31T10:00:52-04:00">
						October 31, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-10-27T12:02:13-04:00">
						October 27, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/5-types-of-imagination-that-take-you-away-from-reality#comments">17 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/5-types-of-imagination-that-take-you-away-from-reality">
						<img width="1060" height="675" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-1060x675.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-1060x675.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-300x191.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-1024x652.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-768x489.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-1536x979.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-2048x1305.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-550x350.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-785x500.jpg 785w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-1920x1223.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-1695x1080.jpg 1695w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/imagination-fiction-fantasy-600x382.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>I have an overactive imagination. Not an hour of the day goes by when I don&#8217;t insert myself into a future that is not yet realized. Such a faculty may be useful for some aspects of creative work, but most of my fantasies are not directed on a specific outcome. Instead, I&#8217;m led astray by my imaginative faculty when I&#8217;m trying to undertake normal tasks like reading, writing, or listening, and it regularly distracts me when I should be serving God with zeal and vigor. I&#8217;m often in a fantasy land that creates an escape from my Christian duties.</p>
<p>What is imagination? Unlike a distinct memory, a relic of something that has already happened, an imagination (or fantasy) is something that has not yet been realized in material existence. You are using your mind to conjure a scene, situation, or outcome that&#8212;at the current moment&#8212;is fiction. Therefore, imagination is future-oriented, whereas a memory, whether enjoyable or not, is past-oriented. Your ability to recall memories is limited by the fixed limitation of memories, but with imagination, there is no limit to what you can invoke. Taken to the extreme, imagination may lead to a complete break from reality.</p>
<p>Orthodox <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/teachings-of-the-church-fathers">Church Fathers</a> state that imagination comes from the <em>nous</em>, which is the eye of the soul. The more damaged your soul, and the further you are from Lord Jesus Christ, the worse your fantasies will be, to the point where they cause you to sin and completely intrude on the ability to have a normal adult life.</p>
<blockquote><p>imagination is one of the faculties of the soul that plays an important role in the action and development of passions. It forms the image of a person or thing within us, then provokes sensual pleasure to capture our nous. Once taken captive we commit sin.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Since the Fall man&#8217;s imaginative faculty has run wild and is full of fantasies. Apart from man, the devil also has imagination. For precisely this reason fantasy and imagination are an efficient conductor of satanic energy and the devil uses them to ensnare people. Fantasy and imagination are a bridge between man and the demons, which the demons cross to trouble him.</p>
<p>&#8212;<a href="https://thoughtsintrusive.wordpress.com/2013/02/12/the-imaginative-faculty-fantasy-imagination/">Metropolitan Hierotheos of Nafpaktos</a></p></blockquote>
<p>When classifying imagination, I noticed two variables that determine the severity of one&#8217;s disconnection from reality. The first variable is the proximity of the fantasy. Does it take place in the next hour or does it take place in a faraway future? The second variable is the likelihood that the fantasy will happen. Are you imagining the conversation you will have with your friend as you are driving to his home or are you fantasizing about being a world-famous singer? If the imagined event is proximal and likely to happen, your fantasy can possibly be described as a rehearsal, but if it is distant and not likely to happen, your fantasy may be a dangerous form of delusion.</p>
<p>Here are five types of imagination that I have noticed myself doing&#8230;</p>
<h3>1. Things right about to happen</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16061" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/job-interview-male-woman.jpg 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>A type of imagination that I&#8217;ve never heard labeled as dangerous is rehearsing for an event that will soon happen. Examples include same-day preparation for a speech, job interview, sporting performance, work meeting, or difficult conversation with a spouse. You mentally arrange the pieces of what is right about to happen to increase the likelihood of success. Such imagination may include logistical planning, dry runs, and scheduling.</p>
<p>To write this article, I had to imagine various ideas and test them in my mind before committing them to paper. My imagination was focused, deliberate, practical, and based on a reality that I wanted to perform. Most jobs require this mode of imagination.</p>
<p>One limitation of this type of imagination is when conversing with others. If you already prepare what you&#8217;re going to say to someone, or what advice you&#8217;re going to give, you may neglect to listen to new information or perceive the shifting needs of the listener and end up speaking at them instead of with them. It&#8217;s easy to turn spontaneous conversations into a lecture through excessive rehearsal and planning.</p>
<h3>2. Things that are likely to happen soon</h3>
<p>We now extend the timeline to things that are planned for the future but which may not happen. Last year, I was booked for a speaking event in Atlanta. I drafted a speech with the expectation I would deliver it, and imagined speaking before the crowd, but the event was cancelled by multiple venues. Another time, I planned to visit my friend <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/11-things-i-learned-from-living-on-the-blue-ridge-mountains-for-2-months">in the mountains</a>. I imagined some topics I was going to talk to him about, but my car broke down and I could not go. Another time, I imagined making vegan banana pancakes and the joy I would get from eating them, but my mom ate all the bananas and I could not make them.</p>
<p>In this category, we&#8217;re starting to see a failure in the realization of our imaginations, even though the failure is unexpected. After all, you did expect the event to occur, and wanted to be prepared for it. I wonder if the most useful aspect of our imaginative faculty is simply helping us prepare for common tasks so that we can give and receive the most spiritual value from them.</p>
<h3>3. Things that are unlikely to happen anytime soon</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16062" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-superhero-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<blockquote><p>The more spiritually sick a person is, the more he is dominated by all kinds of fantasy and imagination. The healthier he is spiritually, the freer he is from fantasies and imaginings. Even what are referred to nowadays as psychological problems are produced and retained in our souls by fantasies. The more we are freed from their oppression, the more we are healed from various psychological problems. This is why St John Cassian the Roman writes that a sign that someone has acquired the virtue of holiness and chastity is that his soul pays no attention at all to imagination or fantasy, even when asleep. &#8212;Ibid</p></blockquote>
<p>With this category, we&#8217;re beginning to escape from reality, because we imagine things that&#8212;even if realized&#8212;won&#8217;t happen for a long time. There becomes a huge gap between the present time and when the fantasy can occur. For example, a man may meet a pretty woman and then later imagine her as his wife, or what it would be like to be intimate with her. A woman may get a haircut and imagine a handsome man who will sweep her off her feet because he <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/worldy-beauty-vs-graceful-beauty">finds her so ravishing</a>. An unemployed computer programmer may imagine being a top executive at a prestigious firm. A single woman may imagine the names of her future children and how beautiful they will be.</p>
<p>Pleasure has begun to seep into the fantasy. The fantasizer disconnects from a boring reality and imagines a future that is pleasurable and more gratifying on the ego, just like how a drug addict ingests a drug to go somewhere else with his mind and body. He doesn&#8217;t like how his life is at the current moment so he imagines a better one in the future, which in turn causes him to neglect the present reality.</p>
<p>Prevalent are fantasies of the flesh. Unfortunately, I have spent untold hours with these types of fantasies in my secular days, which enabled my addiction to carnal living. The fantasies become the main fuel to engage in lawlessness. Fantasies can also exist on the complete opposite end of the spectrum where you imagine catastrophes, traumas, and other bad events that lead to anxiety, despondency, and despair, feelings that tear you away from the Lord.</p>
<h3>4. Lofty fantasies that will <em>never</em> happen</h3>
<blockquote><p>Since the greatest and most terrible passion of all is pride, fantasy and imagination are closely linked with pride. Someone who is proud has something wrong with his imaginative faculty. It is inflamed. It conceives all kinds of images and fantasies and makes his soul an earthquake zone. &#8212;Ibid</p></blockquote>
<p>The previous category had a <em>shred</em> of connection to reality, but now the fantasies become completely void of realism. For example, a man may imagine himself as president of a great empire while deliberating all the excellent laws he should pass, maybe even writing them down. Another man may imagine himself as a hero in a train accident, where his actions save dozens of lives. A woman may imagine herself as a saint who lived centuries ago. A timid man may imagine telling off a politician or policeman to a cheering crowd. A woman may imagine herself as inventing a cure for cancer and winning the Nobel Prize. These fantasies usually involve receiving adoration from a mob, absolute power, or a level of worldwide fame for nonexistent talents or virtues.</p>
<p>I admit that I have delved into this category more often than I like to admit. My insane pride has effortlessly led me to exalted fantasies where I was placed above all men to receive rapturous attention from the most beautiful women in the world. Someone can be especially prone to these fantasies if they are &#8220;bored&#8221; with their lives and want to add excitement or ego gratification without ever leaving their computer chair.</p>
<p>Ultimately, this category of imagination allows a person to believe that they are someone they&#8217;re not. Their entitlement grows and they begin to detach from reality. They fail to empathize with those who are &#8220;beneath&#8221; them in their fantasies, and in heightened states of delusion, they may actually believe their fantasies are truth. If you are experiencing this level of imagination, your soul has likely experienced heavy damage <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/secular-success-vs-christian-success">from secular life</a>.</p>
<h3>5. Vivid dreams, visions, and outright delusion</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16063" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-fantasy-delusion-fog-shadow-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<blockquote><p>Dreams are fantasies, and they relate to the passions existing within us. From the images in these fantasies we can discern which passions we have.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>It is noticeable that studying the writings of the holy Fathers crucifies the imagination, whereas reading impassioned writings, especially fiction, excites the imagination. The Fathers never concerned themselves with so-called Christian fiction, narrative tales and so on, because that sort of writing provokes fantasy. By contrast, even poetry written by the saints has an element of repentance and theoria of God. The poems of St Symeon the New Theologian contain a revelation of God. There is no trace in them of speculation or contamination with figments of the imagination.</p>
<p>&#8212;Ibid</p></blockquote>
<p>If you&#8217;re regularly imagining yourself as a king or queen, chances are you have vivid dreams that further reinforce the belief that you are special, different, or better than others. The cycle becomes self-perpetuating: vivid dreams at night beget crazier fantasies during the day, begetting even more vivid dreams that you want to believe as truth or see as prophecies. More and more of your time is spent outside of reality to the point where you essentially have a second personality that none of your relatives or friends would recognize. You may be an office worker but, according to your imagination, you are an illustrious figure who is not &#8220;understood&#8221; by the common people you interact with. In such a stage of delusion, you buy your own hype and will almost certainly be humbled in a way that will cause despair, when how you see yourself is not confirmed but what life&#8217;s mirror displays.</p>
<p>The imaginative faculty can be so damaged that some people can experience disassociated hallucinogenic states and visions while awake without the use of drugs. In other words, they dream while awake. In extreme conditions, medical treatment may be required, which often requires <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/modern-psychiatry-is-demonic">doping the patient</a> to turn down the biological activity of the brain.</p>
<p><strong>Conclusion</strong></p>
<p>Outside of sensible rehearsing for upcoming events, I don&#8217;t see any positive use of being taken hostage by my imaginative faculty at times when I should be focused on other tasks. The fact that random fantasies come to me when I&#8217;m attempting to serve God, such as while praying or attending a Liturgy, tells me that imagination is more of an <em>intrusion</em> upon my mind instead of an aid. If I want to write <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/heaven-or-hell">a short story</a>, I will sit down and direct my imagination onto the story, but more commonly it seems that my imagination is directing me into strange places and ideas. Before, I would play with fantasies and use them to help me escape the meaningless of life, but since I have found meaning in Christ, I have little use for the games that my imagination wants to play. Unfortunately, I damaged my nous to such an extent from so many years of secular life that I must now battle with this problem daily to attend to my obligations before God.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-salvation-of-your-soul-is-not-a-game"><em><strong>The Salvation Of Your Soul Is Not A Game</strong></em></a></p>
										</div> <!-- .entry-content -->
																			</article>
																	<article id="post-16043" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-16043 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-culture category-faith">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/7-signs-youre-in-a-cult-or-false-movement">7 Signs You&#8217;re In A Cult Or False Movement</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/culture" rel="category tag">Culture</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/7-signs-youre-in-a-cult-or-false-movement" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-10-24T10:00:12-04:00">
						October 24, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-10-19T10:44:10-04:00">
						October 19, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/7-signs-youre-in-a-cult-or-false-movement#comments">34 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/7-signs-youre-in-a-cult-or-false-movement">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-yoga-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>I recently listened to Father John Valdez&#8217;s 10-part lecture series called <a href="https://www.sttimothy.net/index.php/2020/08/13/survival-course-for-orthodox-christians/">Survival Course for Orthodox Christians</a>, which offers a renewed take on Father Seraphim Rose&#8217;s lecture series <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-orthodox-survival-course-by-father-seraphim-rose">of the same name</a>. The talk on Eastern cults was especially helpful because Father John gave a list of signs that one has been deceived by a cult or false movement. I couldn&#8217;t help but notice that I had fallen for most of them to some degree in my secular past. Using Father John&#8217;s lecture as a starting point, I&#8217;d like to share seven of those signs with more detail.</p>
<h3>1. The rules don&#8217;t apply to the guru</h3>
<p>In all cults and false movements, Lord Jesus Christ is either discarded or used as a nominal head, but the real head is a guru who prescribes a litany of rules and commandments for his adherents to follow. The only problem is that the leader has a hard time following his own rules. The excuse of his &#8220;transcendence&#8221; will often be used to exempt him from the group&#8217;s moral teachings, since he will be &#8220;above&#8221; all rules, as if he were a god.</p>
<p>Guru Alan Watts taught a detachment from the world, viciously attacking the Western rat race, yet he was an alcoholic. Osho also taught detachment, yet he was attached to luxury European brands and sexual intercourse with his followers. Many Protestant leaders teach sexual morality, yet they all become embroiled in sex scandals. A worthy leader should follow the rules that he teaches, but that&#8217;s not what happens when a guru teaches a false gospel.</p>
<h3>2. There is no external need for God</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16045" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-1024x680.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="471" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-1024x680.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-300x199.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-768x510.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-1536x1020.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-2048x1361.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-1060x704.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-550x365.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-753x500.jpg 753w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-1920x1275.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-1626x1080.jpg 1626w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-yoga-india-600x399.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>In a false movement, without the guru, you&#8217;re lost. He&#8217;s not directing your soul to God but onto himself so that he gets all the rewards. Since <em>all</em> cults are sex cults in disguise, this means more fleshly rewards for him along with wealth, fame, and riches. The movement manipulates its adherents to think that they are lost without the leader. Guru co-dependency is encouraged.</p>
<p>In Eastern philosophies, a big lie is added: &#8220;You are God.&#8221; The gurus insist that you are perfect, already a literal god, and only need the guru&#8217;s guidance to unlock the divinity within you. This notion is pleasing to <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/do-you-exempt-yourself-from-gods-law">the pride of Western man</a>, who flock towards these teachings to be constantly reminded that they are of the divine and do not have to heal their fallen nature through the grace of God upon repentance.</p>
<h3>3. The promise of fast results without strenuous labor</h3>
<blockquote><p>The striving to defeat the qualities of the fallen nature inspires the monk to such asceticism that those who have never attempted it cannot even imagine. This labor, which is a rejection of one&#8217;s very nature, supplements the crucifixion and cross of poverty, which is only a rejection of money. This labor leads one to the very depth of humility, it brings one to living faith, it raises one to a state of grace. &#8212;Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov in The Field</p></blockquote>
<p>The key to hooking someone onto a false movement is quickly giving them a positive experience that shows the guru&#8217;s teachings &#8220;work&#8221; without having to expend much labor. This type of fast-food spirituality is often done with other adherents who are enraptured by the alleged bliss, peace, or pseudo-grace they are experiencing, enough for the law of social conformity to take over so that the inquirer eagerly misinterprets his feelings as empirical proof of efficacy.</p>
<p>Just meditate for 20 minutes in the way the guru says and you will feel sublime calm. Just attend the rock star church service and you will be buzzing with the Holy Spirit. Just watch all the people falling down in ecstasy before the guru&#8217;s feet and you will feel ecstasy as well if you collapse like the others. Even these kinds of paltry labor are becoming too onerous for modern man, who wants more exalted spiritual experiences with even less work. This has led to the rampant use of drugs, <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/an-orthodox-examination-of-my-foolish-psychedelic-experience">especially psychedelics</a>. Under the guru&#8217;s guidance, you will smoke a potent weed in a hot room, or take mushrooms, and you&#8217;ll feel such peace and maybe even encounter demonic creatures you are told are your pals. You are indebted to the guru for such a mystical journey and commit yourself to him.</p>
<h3>4. Guru rediscovered ancient wisdom that was &#8220;lost&#8221;</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16046" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-1536x1025.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-2048x1367.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-749x500.jpg 749w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-1920x1281.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-1618x1080.jpg 1618w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/indian-male-guru-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>The guru refuses to accept canonical teachings and instead looks for obscure sources to pour in his will and judgment. Osho wrote a book on the Gospel Of Thomas, a non-canonical Gospel, and used it to affirm his own ideas, even blaspheming that Lord Jesus Christ received his teachings from Indian mystics. Many Gnostics on YouTube accept historical speculation as fact to push their own teachings which ultimately reject Orthodox Christology. Protestants read the scripture with their fallen minds and become their own pope, claiming that the teachings of Christ were lost from the time of the Apostles until lawyers and apostate monks enflamed with sexual desire rediscovered them in the 16th Century.</p>
<p>The truth is that since the time of Christ, the truth has never been hidden or lost, because Lord Jesus Christ promised us that His Church would not fall, and through <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-is-orthodox-christianity">the Orthodox Church</a>, it has not.</p>
<h3>5. The familiar is used to build instant rapport</h3>
<p>In modern hip-hop music, it&#8217;s common for a producer to sample an old song and blend it with new degenerate lyrics. This is done so that you feel an instant connection with the new song even though you&#8217;ve never heard it before. False movements do the same by incorporating popular trends existing in the culture so that you quickly feel comfortable in new environs where you must begin to obey the guru. Another example is the similarity between the production values of a rock concert and megachurch. Both use advanced video and audio technology alongside programmatic laser lights. If you want to go to a free rock concert, they occur all around the United States on Sunday mornings.</p>
<blockquote><p>Millennium &#8217;73 was a three-day festival held on November 810, 1973 at the Astrodome in Houston, Texas, United States, by the Divine Light Mission (DLM). It featured Prem Rawat, then known as Guru Maharaj Ji, a 15-year-old guru and the leader of a fast-growing new religious movement. Organizers billed the festival as the most significant event in human history which would usher in a thousand years of peace. The festival&#8217;s official schedule described the three evening addresses by Guru Maharaj Ji as the highlights of the event. <strong>Big-band music, rock bands, religious songs, choral works, a dance performance and speeches by other DLM leaders filled the program from noon to 10 pm.</strong> &#8212;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Millennium_'73">Millenium &#8217;73 event in Houston</a> featuring an Indian child who many thought was god</p></blockquote>
<p>It&#8217;s difficult to find a false movement that is traditional or critical of modern trends because that would <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/10-reasons-why-you-should-visit-an-orthodox-monastery">involve real ascesis</a> that sends the adherent to the true source of traditionalism: Orthodoxy. Instead, the guru must use secular features to hook people into quickly making the decision to become a member so that the fleecing can begin.</p>
<h3>6. There is no objective morality or truth</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16047" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/yoga-class-club.jpg 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<blockquote><p>No one has rightly sought the truth who has not encountered at the end of this search&#8212;whether to accept or reject Him&#8212;our Lord, Jesus Christ, &#8216;the Way, the Truth, and the Life.&#8217; &#8212;Father Seraphim Rose in <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/nihilists-are-spiritually-dead">Nihilism</a></p></blockquote>
<p>The main method to retain members is through the management of their feelings (i.e. emotional manipulation), but since feelings and moods change, the teachings and lessons must also change to keep the coffers filled. This method of control is incompatible with objective truth, which does not change. Since false movements are more concerned with retaining dues-paying members and sex partners, the guru will mold the program so that there is continual growth, as if it were a business.</p>
<p>In the Orthodox Church, if you don&#8217;t want to believe in <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-law-of-god">one of its dogmas</a>, you are outside of the Church. The hierarchy does not soften its stand on a dogma or begin to change because you believe strongly about a lie. Your feelings have absolutely no value when it comes to Church teachings. Compare that with the &#8220;seeker sensitive&#8221; approach of some Protestant churches, whereby a prospective member&#8217;s needs are identified and catered to so that they fill the pews and open their wallet. It&#8217;s possible to be in a modern church and have everyone believe in different dogmas. The truth no longer becomes important while relativity is openly encouraged. It doesn&#8217;t matter what you believe as long as everyone is on the same &#8220;wavelength&#8221; in helping the guru achieve his self-centered mission.</p>
<h3>7. A snippet of scripture or historical text is taken completely out of proportion</h3>
<blockquote><p>Falsehood is a diabolical trait. He who has assimilated false thoughts has assimilated an attribute of the devil. He has entered into a relationship with the outcast angels; he has made union with God alien to himself and unnatural. He who is a stranger to God is a stranger to salvation. &#8212;Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov</p></blockquote>
<p>Famous Russian author <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/top-10-passages-from-leo-tolstoys-war-peace">Leo Tolstoy</a> went against the Orthodox Church and created an entire heretical movement by misinterpreting what the Bible said about peacemaking. He was eventually excommunicated from the Church but managed to cause immense damage to those who believed his lies.</p>
<p>I suspect that modern gurus are less concerned with the truth than appearing different or unique to hook wayward souls onto their movement. They are eager to provide new exegetical accounts that are absurd on their face, but since man is so far from God, born in iniquities and conceived in sin, he is prone to falling for such lies, and so new cults are continually being made.</p>
<p><strong>Conclusion</strong></p>
<blockquote><p>The Holy Spirit, descended on the apostles on the day of Pentecost, according to the words of the Lord Jesus Christ Himself, who promised to send Him down at the Last Supper, is primarily the Spirit of truth and was sent to the disciples of the Lord in order to instruct them on all truth (Jn 16, 13), and therefore the true Church of Christ, informing the believers of the grace of the Holy Spirit, is the one who keeps, confesses and preaches the Truth. In the same place where, instead of Truth, lies are proclaimed, whether in dogmatic doctrine or in moral or in the sense of any untruth in general, there certainly is no true Church, there is no God&#8217;s grace that saves man, but only one appearance, blasphemous deception. &#8212;<a href="https://archbishopaverky.blogspot.com/2018/03/about-mp.html">Archbishop Averky</a></p></blockquote>
<p>I fell for many of the above tricks when I believed in the Eastern lie of becoming your own God. I believed <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/16-types-of-thoughts-that-assault-me-while-praying">in my thoughts</a> and feelings and essentially did whatever I wanted to do in the name of being one with the Universe and acting as a dead fish to &#8220;go with the flow.&#8221; There was no grace and no healing to my soul. Shamefully, I even went to a couple of yoga classes while living in Europe to mimic bodily configurations that were historically used to commune with Hindu demons. Thankfully, Lord Jesus Christ has removed the scales from my eyes and allowed me to see the full truth&#8212;without adulteration and without error&#8212;through His Orthodox Church. No one converts to Orthodoxy without having sustained prior damage from false movements, so may God help them all be received into the only true movement that is God&#8217;s Church.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/why-do-you-consume-secular-content"><em><strong>Why Do You Consume Secular Content?</strong></em></a></p>

						October 17, 2022					</time>

						October 13, 2022					</time>
				</a>

					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/33-things-christian-men-should-know-about-women#comments">318 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->

														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/33-things-christian-men-should-know-about-women">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-happy-casual-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>A common lament from chaste Orthodox men I meet is their lack of experience in dealing with women who are more socialized than them. How can these men understand women, identify one with strong faith, and make confident decisions concerning marriage? As an unmarried middle-aged man, I stress to them how I&#8217;m not in a better situation, but they nonetheless feel that I can give them profitable lessons in their quest to enter an Orthodox marriage due to my excessive secular experience.</p>
<p>I have tried to be thoughtful about what I&#8217;m about to share so as not to interfere with God&#8217;s will in bringing together man and woman in one flesh within the Church sacrament of marriage, because most of my experiences with women took place sinfully outside of marriage, causing me to lose all manner of healthy child-like innocence when viewing the opposite sex. I do not consider myself bitter, but I am surely cynical from partaking in behaviors that went against the commandments of God for so many years. If you perceive undue pessimism or even anger in my words, it is due to the damage I inflicted upon myself, not because God made a mistake in how he constructed man or woman. If you participate in evil for a prolonged period of time, you will carry distorted views of reality even <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/are-you-on-the-path-to-salvation">long after repentance</a>.</p>
<p>It could be possible that a secular woman you have feelings for will possess every negative trait I&#8217;m about to describe. When a woman lacks spiritual life, she does not struggle against her passions and sins, or even think they are wrong. On the other hand, the Orthodox women I&#8217;ve met and observed possess at least a basic desire for moral goodness, and will automatically be more suitable for marriage. However, some Orthodox women are more zealous than others, and they all swim in a putrid secular fishbowl. The tainted water corrupts us without our conscious awareness, and so it&#8217;s not uncommon for an Orthodox woman to possess deep-seated secular beliefs that can strain a marriage. You must be discerning when it comes to identifying any beliefs that would be detrimental to maintaining a Christian family home.</p>
<p>I will often use the secular word &#8220;game&#8221; in this article. Game is a collection of psychological and behavioral techniques to attract a woman physically and emotionally for the purpose of fornication and fleshly pair bonding. Game includes: approaching an unknown woman in a public place while play-acting as a confident man, optimizing one&#8217;s aesthetic so that it pleases worldly woman, using salesman techniques of rapport building and scarcity to make a fast &#8220;sale,&#8221; hiding flaws while showcasing strengths, deliberately pumping up a woman&#8217;s emotions, lying, omitting the truth, putting a woman in a negative state of anxiety or dread to modulate her attractive feelings, and exploiting a woman&#8217;s human weaknesses for selfish gain.</p>
<p>In the game process, <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/game-is-for-fallen-women">God is absent</a>, and the primary goal of the man is to satisfy his selfish craving for positive female attention, worldly love, and physical pleasure. Even if you claim to desire abstinence before marriage, you can still be using game by implementing secular techniques to meet women, get their phone number, arrange dates, and so on. A sign you are <em>not</em> using game is if you adhere to the old clich &#8220;be yourself,&#8221; where yourself is a child of God who follows His commandments with the understanding that marriage is a sacrament whose purpose is to usher two souls into heaven. The Christian way is to trust in God to pair you with a woman who is on your social and spiritual level instead of pretending to be an alpha male to deceive a woman into liking you using mostly physical and psychological means.</p>
<p>That said, here is a list of general guidance for men who want to pick the right woman for marriage in an Orthodox courtship where the man clearly expresses to the woman beforehand that no intimacy can take place until they are united in one flesh through the Church sacrament of marriage.</p>
<h3>1. Assume that you will never change her</h3>
<blockquote><p>Who can find a virtuous wife? For her worth is far above rubies. The heart of her husband safely trusts her; So he will have no lack of gain. She does him good and not evil all the days of her life. &#8212;Proverbs 31:10-12</p></blockquote>
<p>It&#8217;s a fatal temptation for a man to look at a woman, especially a young one, as a <em>tabula rasa</em>, a blank slate for him to mold into his perfect, traditional wife who bakes cookies and croissants all day. Such a man sees all her flaws and thinks that, with time, he can eradicate them one by one as if using a laser beam. Or he sees her annoying personality traits and thinks that he can dampen them with a sort of punishment-reward stratagem. This is delusion. Who she is is who she is, and if she does change, it will be entirely dependent on her own will and its cooperation with God to serve the good. Any immediate change you do see in her, without much in the way of effort, should be viewed with suspicion.</p>
<p>Do you know how hard it is to change a single behavior, personality trait, or quirk? For example, I have the bad habit of taking the Lord&#8217;s name in vain by saying the word &#8220;Jeez&#8221; as an exclamation. For a couple of months, I have tried mightily to stop using this term, but I have not yet been successful. I have a bad habit of eating past 8pm. I&#8217;m grumpy in the mornings. I&#8217;m overly sensitive to noise and odors. I prefer socializing only in the evening. I have innumerable preferences that a potential wife may not like and will try to change, but chances are she will fail until Im enlightened by God to work harder at correction not for my sake but for the sake of the marriage.</p>
<p>Through God&#8217;s grace, I&#8217;ve been able to step away from sinful behaviors, but the little things that are entrenched into my personality, and which do not pose an immediate risk to my salvation, have remained. This is also the case with women. Do not assume you will change her. Do not assume you can even get her to grow her hair an inch longer than it already is. Do not assume she will change <em>at all</em>. Of course a woman will do many things to please her man, such as to lose a few pounds or dress differently, and she may be motivated to improve for you in a way that she didn&#8217;t while single, but dont expect immediate, permanent change.</p>
<h3>2. Women are capable of deceiving men</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16023" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/male-woman-date-skeptical-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<blockquote><p>An excellent wife is the crown of her husband, But she who causes shame is like rottenness in his bones.<br />
&#8212;Proverbs 12:4</p></blockquote>
<p>The more secular a woman is, the more likely she will set out to deceive a man without ever believing she is being deceptive. How this plays out is that everything will seem to be going well with her while in a romantic relationship, and then one day you are blindsided by her shocking behavior. I wrote books on women, thought I knew them better than myself, but was still badly deceived by them, because as a man, we are not given natural tools to spot every female deception under the sun. There are thousandsperhaps millions of menwho came home one day and stumbled upon a horrible discovery that changed their lives forever. In heartache, they concluded that they never really knew their significant other at all.</p>
<p>Its possible for a woman to pretend to be someone she is not, sometimes for many years and certainly for the short amount of time needed to put forth a favorable impression and cement a man&#8217;s affections during courtship. I&#8217;ve seen it with my own eyes. Depending on how skilled she is, the lie may be something as minor as a political opinion she&#8217;s hiding to not displease you or as serious as living an entirely different lifestyle behind your back. The man who is lusting after a woman will not be able to see through the deception, but a chaste man whose eyes and ears are not tainted by lust should be able to see through any false faade by picking up on inconsistencies in behavior while continually self-checking whether she is &#8220;too good to be true.&#8221;</p>
<p>At the risk of getting philosophical, I believe that women themselves dont know when theyre being deceptive or not. Their behavior is subconsciously driven to maximize the rewards received from a man with whom they want to be in a relationship. On the other hand, it is unlikely that a woman is consciously deceiving you if she is open about confessing all her flaws and problems.</p>
<h3>3. If her spirit and behavior are more secular than Orthodox, she is abiding by the secular world</h3>
<blockquote><p>Wisdom rests in the heart of him who has understanding, But what is in the heart of fools is made known. &#8212;Proverbs 14:33</p></blockquote>
<p>A fish may strongly desire to be a healthy fish, but if it&#8217;s swimming in polluted water, many of its biological functions will be impaired. As sincerely as we wish to be Orthodox, the waters around us are dirty and foul, and though our intentions may be good, we simply cannot block out all the toxic effects that are seeping unaware into our souls. I believe that even listening to one pop song can be damaging to the soul, and yet if we don&#8217;t voluntarily listen to such music, we are subjected to it every time we <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/why-does-the-supermarket-play-pop-music">walk into a retail store</a>.</p>
<p>It&#8217;s great that a woman goes to Liturgy every Sunday and confesses her sins and receives Communion, but it is not great if for the six remaining days of the week she is glued to her smartphone, watches Netflix, attends a university, listens to rap music, reads feminist influencers online, uses TikTok, watches reality television, follows celebrity gossip, and participates in Snapchat exchanges with men. In such a case, her behavior will be more driven by secular trends than her faith, driving her away from traditional family life.</p>
<p>If I met a woman who consumed over 20 hours of secular content a week, but spent only 5 hours on her faith, yet proclaimed to me that she wants to be a traditional wife, I would think she&#8217;s confused, because it&#8217;s not traditional to be <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/why-do-you-consume-secular-content">attached to worldly content</a> streamed from her smartphone. If, however, another woman said she wants to be traditional, and shares a sentiment of hatred toward the modern world, and I can hardly get in touch with her because she leaves her smartphone off for most of the day, I can be more assured that she is sincere.</p>
<p>Since a woman&#8217;s smartphone is an extension of her personality and innermost desires, I may ask any female I&#8217;m considering if she can show me all the apps installed on her phone. If she has all the popular social media apps, and not even a single Bible or prayer app, you have an answer.</p>
<p>Just because a woman is Orthodox does not mean you must throw away all discernment and think everything will be fine. She is still a product of this corrupt world and you must keep your wits about you to see if she possesses the most important qualities needed to be a wife and mother. You must examine her flaws and ask yourself if you can endure them, and ask if your flaws can be endured by her. You don&#8217;t want a woman exclaiming &#8220;I&#8217;m Orthodox&#8221; to cause you to close your eyes and jump in without discernment.</p>
<h3>4. A woman who maintains a perfect physical appearance may crave validation from men more than God</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16024" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-model-makeup-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<blockquote><p>And there a woman met him, with the attire of a harlot, and a crafty heart. She was loud and rebellious, her feet would not stay at home. At times she was outside, at times in the open square, lurking at every corner. &#8212;Proverbs 7:10-12</p></blockquote>
<p>It is my experience that the more time a woman invests into her external appearance, the less time she invests in the internal (her soul). This was most vividly shared with me during my long-ago stint in Ukraine, which had the most beautiful women out of all the nations I&#8217;ve visited. Part of their beauty was natural, as the beauty of Slavic women is renowned, but much of it is time spent on manual physical enhancement at the beauty salon.</p>
<p>On my dates with Ukrainian women, they revealed to me how much time they spend on their hair, nails, makeup, skin, clothing, and so on, and yet those same women could not tell me the last book they read. It turned out that I&#8212;as an impassioned foreign tourist&#8212;was selecting the most materialistic women in Ukraine who wanted to trade their beauty for an increase in adventure or living standard. Consider that these women spent a huge percentage of their low incomes simply on beauty upkeep, which in hindsight was depressing because Ukraine is an Orthodox country with God&#8217;s bottomless grace available to them if they walked around the corner of their home into a church. I enabled their materialistic behavior by giving them my attention, interest, affection, and time in the hopes of a carnal reward.</p>
<p>Be on guard for a woman who has <em>excessive</em> concern for her appearance, because that may signify that her flesh is getting more maintenance than her soul. That will be a large problem for a passionate secular man who marries her, because a woman&#8217;s vanity may only please his eyes for a short period of time.</p>
<h3>5. You will not choose a woman with wisdom if your passions are elevated</h3>
<blockquote><p>With her enticing speech she caused him to yield, with her flattering lips she seduced him. Immediately he went after her, as an ox goes to the slaughter, or as a fool to the correction of the stocks, till an arrow struck his liver. As a bird hastens to the snare, he did not know it would cost his life. Proverbs 7:21-23</p></blockquote>
<p>Passions are fleeting, temporary, and capricious. Making life decisions based on your passions and emotional urges is like building a house on sand. If a passionate woman likes you, it is more likely because you please her physically and emotionally in the current moment, not because she has assessed your faith and values for the long term. Passionate secular men, of which I was one, want to be pleased in the moment. They think that every flight of fancy that enters their mind is a worthwhile pursuit that can maximize their happiness. It was my unbridled passion that allowed me to waste two decades of my life, selecting the wrong women continually for bodily pleasure, pride, and masculine ego gratification. I had built my whole life on sand and realized at a late hour what a folly that was.</p>
<p>If you meet a woman you like, and for the next few days you can&#8217;t even think straight because your mind is whirring with fantasies about how beautiful she is and how great your future life will be and how many children you will have, you are aflame with passion and emotion. Even adrenaline may be at play if you find it hard to sleep because of thoughts concerning her. This behavior is actually feminine, codified in hundreds of romance novels. We are men, not women, and must check ourselves when we enter &#8220;romance novel&#8221; mode, of which I have done innumerable times.</p>
<p>It&#8217;s safer instead to make a more detached assessment that allows logic to reign so that you can build any future relationship on rock instead of sand. One sign you are proceeding correctly is if you&#8217;re patient and take your time to evaluate a woman before even speaking with her. If there is a woman in my church who I&#8217;m interested in, I will not immediately strain to talk to her. Instead, I will observe her from a distance, politely ask about her situation to married parishioners or church elders (without fishing for gossip), and then contemplate the matter for days or weeks until I can make a calm assessment of whether it&#8217;s even reasonable to have a conversation with her. On the other hand, if I see a new girl in the church and run up to her after the Liturgy with a church pickup line, I&#8217;m simply following my passions.</p>
<p>I am surprised how much pickup culture has infused into the minds of young Orthodox men, but I can tell you that such techniques are a blind alley. You must not be burning with desire when deciding to get to know a new woman.</p>
<h3>6. Beware if &#8220;game&#8221; works on her</h3>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-16025" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/woman-date-seduction-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
