										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-happens-to-your-soul-after-you-die">What Happens To Your Soul After You Die</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/book-reviews" rel="category tag">Book Reviews</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/orthodoxy" rel="category tag">Orthodoxy</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-happens-to-your-soul-after-you-die" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-10-10T10:00:45-04:00">
						October 10, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-10-05T11:31:00-04:00">
						October 5, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-happens-to-your-soul-after-you-die#comments">50 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-happens-to-your-soul-after-you-die">
						<img width="1060" height="689" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-1060x689.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-1060x689.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-300x195.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-1024x666.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-768x499.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-550x358.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-769x500.jpg 769w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses-600x390.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/Russian-Orthodox-Icon-Toll-Houses.jpg 1172w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Soul-After-Death-Seraphim-Rose/dp/093863514X?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=cea994ebdb79104879501bacb34550a2&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-14912" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/book-soulafter.jpg" alt="" width="70" height="110" /></a></p>
<p><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Soul-After-Death-Seraphim-Rose/dp/093863514X?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=cea994ebdb79104879501bacb34550a2&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">The Soul After Death</a> by Father Seraphim Rose shares the Orthodox Christian position on what happens to human beings upon death. Father Seraphim reviews the teachings of saints to explain modern phenomena such as near-death experiences of those who have been revived after clinical death and also out-of-body experiences among psychedelic drug users. His book is critical reading for serious Christians, because if one were to subscribe to errant beliefs about death, and come to think that &#8220;everybody goes to heaven&#8221; or that &#8220;heaven is a state of mind, not a place,&#8221; it will start to negatively affect their spiritual life and may ultimately lead to eternal condemnation.</p>
<h4>What is death?</h4>
<blockquote><p>Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov: &#8220;By the fall both the soul and body of man were changed. In the strict sense the fall was for them also a death. That which we see and call death is in essence only the separation of the soul from the body, both of which had already before this been put to death by an eternal death!&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>Do you believe in a spiritual reality?</h4>
<blockquote><p>We who live on earth can hardly even begin to understand the reality of the spiritual world until we ourselves come to dwell in it. This is a process that begins now, in this life, but ends only in eternity, when we will behold &#8220;face to face&#8221; what we now see only &#8220;through a glass, darkly&#8221; (1 Cor. 13:12).</p></blockquote>
<p>If you don&#8217;t believe in a spiritual reality then everything you do will be structured around pleasing your body and flesh until you die, and then when you die, none of that body-pleasing will be useful when you are fully aware and present in soul to be judged by God.</p>
<h4>What can we learn from near-death experiences among heterodox and non-Christians?</h4>
<blockquote><p>Dr. Kubler-Ross mentions one remarkable case where a blind person &#8220;saw&#8221; and later described everything clearly in the room where she &#8220;died,&#8221; although when she came back to life she was once again blind&#8212;a striking evidence that it is not the eye that sees (not the brain that thinks, for the mental faculties become quicker after death), but rather the <em>soul</em> that performs these actions <em>through</em> the physical organs as long as the body is alive, but <em>by its own power</em> when the body is dead.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>It is characteristic of our times of unbelief that these people seldom use the Christian vocabulary or realize that it is their <em>soul</em> that has been set free from the body and now experiences everything; they are usually simply puzzled at the new state they find themselves in.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>most, perhaps indeed all, of [near-death] experiences have little in common with the Christian vision of heaven. These visions are not spiritual, but <em>worldly</em>. They are so quick, so easily attained, so common, so earthly in their imagery, that there can be no serious comparison of them with the true Christian visions of heaven in the past Even the most &#8220;spiritual&#8221; thing about some of them&#8212;the feeling of the &#8220;presence&#8221; of Christ&#8212;persuades one more of the spiritual immaturity of those who experience it than of anything else. Rather than producing the profound awe, fear of God, and repentance which the authentic experience of God&#8217;s presence has evoked in Christians saints (of which St. Paul&#8217;s experience on the road to Damascus may be taken as a model&#8212;Acts 9:3-9), the present-day experiences produce something much more akin to the &#8220;comfort&#8221; and &#8220;peace&#8221; of the modern spiritistic and Pentecostal movements.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>[near-death experiences] may be said to &#8220;prove&#8221; no more than a minimum doctrine of the bare survival of the human soul outside the body, and of the bare existence of a non-material reality, while giving decisively no information on non-material reality, while giving decisively no information on the further state of even existence of the soul after the first few minutes of &#8220;death,&#8221; nor of the ultimate nature of the non-material realm.</p></blockquote>
<h4>What does it mean to see dead relatives?</h4>
<blockquote><p>St. Gregory the Great, in describing many of these experiences in Dialogues, explains the phenomenon of meeting others: &#8220;It frequently happens that a soul on the point of death recognizes those with whom it is to share the same eternal dwelling for equal blame or reward&#8221; (Dialogues, IV, 36). And specifically with regard to those who have led a righteous life, St. Gregory notes that &#8220;if often happens that the saints of heaven appear to the righteous at the hour of death in order to reassure them. And, with the vision of the heavenly company before their minds, they die without experiencing any fear of agony&#8221; (Dialogues, IV, 12).</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>These encounters, while they do not seem by any means to occur to everyone before death, still can be called universal in the sense that they occur without regard to nationalist, religion, or holiness of life.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>it must be that the dead relatives who are seen as not actually &#8220;present&#8221; as the dying believe them to be. St. Gregory the Great says only that the dying man &#8220;recognizes&#8221; people, whereas to the righteous &#8220;the saints of heaven appear&#8221;&#8212;a distinction which not merely indicates the different experience of the righteous and ordinary sinners when they die, but also is directly bound up with the different afterlife state of the saints and ordinary sinners. The saints have great freedom to intercede for the living and to come to their aid, whereas deceased sinners, save in very special cases, have no contact with the living.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>we need not doubt that the saints actually appear to the righteous at death, as is described in many Lives of Saints. To ordinary sinners, on the other hand, there are often apparitions of relatives, friends, or &#8220;gods&#8221; which correspond to what the dying either expect or are prepared to see. The exact nature of these latter apparitions it is probably impossible to define; they are certainly not mere hallucinations, but seem to be a part of the natural experience of death, a sign to the dying person (as it were) that he is about to enter a new realm where the laws of ordinary material reality no longer hold. There is nothing very extraordinary about this experience, which seems to hold constant for different times, places, and religions.</p></blockquote>
<h4>Applying discernment to near-death experiences</h4>
<blockquote><p>we must clearly distinguish between genuine, grace-given visions of the other world, and a merely natural experience which, even though it may be outside the normal limits of human experience, is not in the least spiritual and tells us nothing about the actual reality of either the heaven or the hell of authentic Christian teaching.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>One who is aware of this Orthodox teaching cannot but look in amazement and horror at the ease with which contemporary &#8220;Christians&#8221; trust the visions and apparitions which are now becoming so common. The reason for this credulity is clear: Roman Catholicism and Protestantism, cut off for centuries now from the Orthodox doctrine and practice of spiritual life, have lost all capability for clear discernment in the realm of spirits.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Those who are seeing &#8220;paradise&#8221; in the aerial realm today are &#8220;pleased,&#8221; &#8220;happy,&#8221; &#8220;satisfied&#8221;&#8212;seldom anything more; if they behold &#8220;Christ&#8221; in some form, it is only to indulge in the familiar &#8220;dialogues&#8221; with him that characterize experiences in the &#8220;charismatic&#8221; movement. The element of the Divine and of man&#8217;s awe before it, the fear of God, are absent in such experiences.</p></blockquote>
<h4>Demons will tempt you at the time of death and even right after</h4>
<blockquote><p>The Orthodox Lives of Saints have numerous accounts of demonic spectacles which appear at the moment of death, usually with the aim of frightening the dying person and making him despair over his salvation.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>The hour of death, then, is indeed a time of demonic temptation, and the &#8220;spiritual experiences&#8221; which people have at this time are to be subjected to the same standard of Christian teaching as are any other &#8220;spiritual experiences.&#8221; Likewise, the &#8220;spirits&#8221; who may be encountered at this time are to be subjected to the universal test which the Apostle John expresses in the words: Test the spirits, whether they are of God, because many false prophets are gone out into the world (1 John 4:1).</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>It befits us, therefore, to be very suspicious (at the least) of the &#8220;beings of light&#8221; who seem to appear in the moment of death. They seem very much like demons posing as &#8220;angels of light&#8221; in order to seduce, not only the dying person himself, but even more those to whom he will later tell this tale if he is resuscitated (concerning the chances of which, of course, the demons are well aware).</p></blockquote>
<p>The demons are not ignorant that people who are clinically dead may be revived, so it is profitable for them to give people a &#8220;peaceful&#8221; and &#8220;calm&#8221; vision so that, in the case they do come back to life, they will ecstatically share this vision to all, reinforcing the desired notion that everybody goes to heaven and <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-field-of-spiritual-warfare">spiritual labors</a> are not necessary.</p>
<p>Also, don&#8217;t despair if you&#8217;re swarmed by imp-looking demons surrounding your deathbed. You may think that your judgment has arrived, but really it could be a final temptation by Satan for you to forsake God.</p>
<h4>Demons provide a vision at death that corresponds to an individual&#8217;s beliefs</h4>
<blockquote><p>It is not necessary for us to define precisely the nature of the apparitions of the dying in order to see that they depend to some extent, as we have already seen on what the dying person <em>expects</em> or is <em>prepared</em> to see. Thus, Christians of past centuries who had a lively belief in hell, and whose conscience accused them in the end, often saw demons at death; Indians of today, who are certainly more &#8220;primitive&#8221; than Americans in their beliefs and understanding, often see beings that correspond to their still very real fears about the afterlife; while contemporary Americans, with their &#8220;enlightened&#8221; views, see apparitions in harmony with their &#8220;comfortable&#8221; life and beliefs, which in general do not include a very realistic fear of hell or awareness of demons.</p>
<p>On the objective side, the demons themselves offer temptations which accord with the spiritual state or expectations of those being tempted. For those who fear hell, the demons may appear in terrible forms in order to make a person die in a state of despair; but for those who do not believe in hell (or for Protestants who believe they are infallibly &#8220;saved&#8221; and therefore need not fear hell) the demons would naturally offer temptations in some other form that would not so clearly expose their evil intent. Likewise, even to a Christian struggler who has already suffered much, the demons may appear in such a way as to seduce him rather than frighten him.</p></blockquote>
<h4>The activity of demons</h4>
<blockquote><p>Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov: &#8220;The holy spirits avoid communion with men who are unworthy of such communion; while the fallen spirits, who have drawn us into their fall, have mingled with us and, so as the more easily to hold us in captivity, strive to make both themselves and their chains unnoticeable to us. And if they do reveal themselves, they do it in order to strengthen their dominion over us.&#8221;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov: &#8220;the spirits who appear sensuously to men who are in a state of sinfulness and fall, are demons and not in the least holy angels. &#8216;A filthy soul,&#8217; said St. Isaac the Syrian, &#8221;does not enter the pure realm and is not joined to holy spirits&#8217; (Homily 74). Holy angels appear only to holy men who have restored communion with God and with them by a holy life.&#8221;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov: &#8220;The fallen angels are dispersed in a multitude throughout the entire transparent immensity which we see above us. They do not cease to disturb all human societies and every person separately; there is no evil deed, no crime, of which they might not be instigators and participants; they incline and instruct men towards sin by all possible means. <em>Your adversary the devil</em>, says the holy Apostle Peter, <em>walketh about like a roaring lion, seeking whom he may devour</em> (1 Peter 5:8), both during our earthly life and after the separation of the soul from the body. When the soul of a Christian, leaving its earthly dwelling, begins to strive through the aerial spaces towards the homeland on high, the demons stop it, strive to find in it a kinship with themselves, their sinfulness, their fall, and to drag it down to the hell <em>prepared for the devil and his angels</em> (Matt. 25:41). They act thus by the right which they have acquired.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>The foolishness of seeking visions and spiritual experiences</h4>
<blockquote><p>Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov: &#8220;The desire to see spirits, curiosity to find out anything about them and from them, is a sign of the greatest foolishness and total ignorance of the Orthodox Church&#8217;s traditions concerning moral and active life. Knowledge of spirits is acquired quite differently than is supposed by the inexperienced and careless experimenter. Open communion with spirits for the inexperienced is the greatest misfortune, or serves as a source of the greatest misfortunes.&#8221;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov: &#8220;One who perceives spirits sensuously can easily be deceived to his own harm and perdition. If, on perceiving spirits, he shows trust or credulity towards them, he will unfailingly be deceived, he will unfailingly be attracted, he will unfailingly be sealed with the seal of deception, not understandable to the inexperienced, the seal of a frightful injury in his spirit; and further, the possibility of correction and salvation is often lost. This has happened with many, very many.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>Judgment after death</h4>
<blockquote><p>[Concerning] our redemption by Jesus Christ, [Saint Ignatius Brianchaninov says,] &#8220;all who have openly rejected the Redeemer comprise the inheritance of satan: their souls, after the separation from the body, descend straight to hell. But Christians who are inclined to sin are also unworthy of being immediately translated from earthly life to blessed eternity. Justice itself demands that these inclinations to sin, these betrayals of the Redeemer should be weighted and evaluated. A judging and distinguishing are required in order to define the degree of a Christian soul&#8217;s inclination to sin, in order to define what predominates in it&#8212;eternal life or eternal death. The unhypocritical Judgment of God awaits every Christian soul after its departure from the body, as the holy Apostle Paul has said: It is appointed unto men once to die, and after this the judgment (Heb. 9:27).&#8221;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>What is certain is that there <em>is</em> a testing by demons, who appear in a frightful but human form, accuse the newly-departed of sins and literally try to seize the subtle body of the soul, which is grasped firmly by angels; and all this occurs in the air above us and can be seen by those whose eyes are open to spiritual reality.</p></blockquote>
<p>In <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-law-of-god">the Orthodox Church</a>, the initial judgment after death is called the &#8220;particular judgment.&#8221; Prayers can help the dead who have not fared well in this judgment, changing their eternal fate. The final judgment occurs on the Last Day and is, as you may have guessed, final.</p>
<h4>What exactly happens when you die?</h4>
<blockquote><p>St. Cyril: &#8220;What fear and trembling await you, O soul, in the day of death! You will see frightful, wild, cruel, unmerciful and shameful demons, like dark Ethiopians, standing before you. The very sight of them is worse than any torment. The soul, seeing them, becomes agitated, is disturbed, troubled, seeks to hide, hastens to the angels of God. The holy angels hold the soul; passing with them through the air and rising, it encounters the toll-houses which guard the path from earth to heaven, detaining the soul and hindering it from ascending further. Each toll-house tests the sins corresponding to it; each sin, each passion has its tax collectors and testers.&#8221;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>As a sensuous or &#8220;natural&#8221; experience, therefore, it would seem that death is indeed pleasant. This pleasantness may be experienced equally by one whose conscience is clean before God, and by one who does not deeply believe in God or eternal life at all, and therefore has no awareness of how he may have displeased God during his lifetime. A &#8220;bad death&#8221; is experienced, as one writer has well said, only by &#8220;those who know that God exists, and yet have lived their lives as though He did not&#8221;&#8212;i.e., those whose consciences torment them and counteract by their pain the natural &#8220;pleasure&#8221; of physical death. The distinction between believers and unbelievers occurs, then, not at the moment of death itself, but later, at the Particular Judgment. The &#8220;pleasantness&#8221; of death may be real enough, but it has no necessary connection whatever with the eternal fate of the soul, which may well be one of torment.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>In the contemporary experiences the soul is most frequently offered a choice to remain in &#8220;paradise&#8221; or go back to earth; while the genuine experience of heaven occurs not by the choice of man but only at the command of God, fulfilled by His angels. The common &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experience of &#8220;paradise&#8221; in our days has no need of a guide because it takes place right here, in the air above us, still in this world; while the presence of the guiding angels is necessary if the experience takes place outside this world, in a different kind of reality, where the soul cannot go by itself. (This is not to say that demons cannot masquerade as &#8220;guiding angels&#8221; also, but they seldom seem to do so in today&#8217;s experiences.)</p></blockquote>
<p>Secular people are hung up on the delayed inevitability of physical death, and cope by distracting themselves in this life with <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/15-signs-youre-a-dopamine-slave">endless amusements</a> and doctor visits, but it&#8217;s really the potential for spiritual death that we should focus our labors on.</p>
<h4>Death experiences of the Saints</h4>
<blockquote><p>Saint Ignatius: &#8220;The great saints of God pass through the aerial guards of the dark powers with such great freedom because during earthly life they enter into uncompromising battle with them and, gaining the victory over them, acquire in the depths of their heart complete freedom from sin, become the temple and sanctuary of the Holy Spirit, making their rational dwelling-place inaccessible for the fallen angels.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>The aerial realm</h4>
<blockquote><p>The realm into which the soul immediately enters when it leaves the body and begins to lose contact with what we know as &#8220;material reality&#8221; (whether after death or in a simple &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experience) is neither heaven nor hell, but an invisible realm close to earth which is variously called the &#8220;After-death&#8221; or &#8220;Bardo plane&#8221; (Tibetan Book of the Dead), the &#8220;world of spirits&#8221; (Swedenborg and spiritism), the &#8220;astral plane&#8221; (Theosophy and most of occultism), &#8220;Locale II&#8221; (Monroe)&#8212;or, in Orthodox language, the aerial world of the under-heaven where fallen spirits dwell and are active in deceiving men for their damnation. This is not the &#8220;other world&#8221; that awaits man after death, but only the invisible part of <em>this</em> world that man must pass through to reach the truly &#8220;other&#8221; world of heaven or hell. For those who have truly died, and are being conducted by angels out of earthly life, this is the realm where the Particular Judgment begins at the aerial &#8220;toll-houses,&#8221; where the spirits of the air reveal their real nature and their hostility towards mankind; for all others, it is a realm of demonic deception at the hands of these same spirits.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>The beings contacted in this realm are always (or almost always) demons, whether they are invoked by mediumism or other occult practices, or encountered in &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experiences. They are not angels, for these dwell in heaven and only pass through this realm as messengers of God. They are not the souls of the dead, for they dwell in heaven or hell and only pass through this realm immediately after death on their way to judgment for their actions in this life. Even those most adept in &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experiences cannot remain in this realm for long without danger of permanent separation from the body (death)&#8230;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Almost all contemporary researchers accept or at least are highly sympathetic to the occult teaching regarding this realm, for the single reason that it is based on experience, which is also the basis of science. But &#8220;experience&#8221; in the material world is something quite different from &#8220;experience&#8221; in the aerial realm. The raw material being experienced and studied in the one case is morally &#8220;neutral,&#8221; and it can be studied objectively and verified by others; but in the other case the &#8220;raw material&#8221; is hidden, extremely difficult to grasp, and, in many cases, has a will of its own&#8212;a will to deceive the observer.</p></blockquote>
<h4>What is really going on with modern near-death experiences?</h4>
<blockquote><p>The passage through the toll-houses&#8212;which is a kind of touchstone of authentic after-death experience&#8212;is not described at all in today&#8217;s experiences, and the reason for this is not far to seek. From many signs&#8212;the absence of the angels who come for the soul, the absence of judgment, the frivolousness of many of the accounts, even the very shortness of the time involved (usually some five to ten minutes, compared with the several hours to several days in the incidents from saint&#8217; Lives and other Orthodox sources)&#8212;it is clear that today&#8217;s experiences, although sometimes very striking and not explainable by any natural laws known to medical science, are not very profound. If these are actual experiences of death, then they involve only the very beginning of the soul&#8217;s after-death journey; they occur in the anteroom of death, as it were, before God&#8217;s decree for the soul has become final (manifested by the coming of the angels for the soul), while there is still a possibility for the soul to return to the body by natural means.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>It is not precisely an &#8220;after-death&#8221; experience; it is rather the &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experience which is only the antechamber to other much more extensive experiences, whether of death itself or of what is sometimes called &#8220;astral travelling&#8221; Although the &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; state might be called the &#8220;first moment&#8221; of death&#8212;if death actually follows&#8212;it is a gross mistake to conclude from it anything whatever about the &#8220;after-death&#8221; state, unless it be the bare facts of the survival and consciousness of the soul after death, which hardly anyone who actually believes in the soul&#8217;s immortality denies in any case.</p></blockquote>
<p>There is an aerial realm above us that we cannot see because our spiritual eyes are shut. This aerial realm is infested with demons. When you die, your soul launches into the aerial realm for a brief period, where the demons can influence you with various visions, until the holy angels come down to begin your trial of particular judgment. Many <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/an-orthodox-examination-of-my-foolish-psychedelic-experience">psychedelic drugs</a> have the ability to put you in the aerial realm where what you see is almost certainly a demonic trick. Proof of this is the fact that very few psychedelic users interpret their &#8220;spiritual experiences&#8221; of the aerial realm in a way that steers them into the Orthodox Church. The vast majority fall back into a variety of pantheistic, gnostic, deistic, or New Age belief systems that are not sufficient for salvation.</p>
<h4>It is pleasing for the soul to separate from a body corrupted with sins</h4>
<blockquote><p>Our physical bodies in this fallen world are bodies of pain, corruption, and death. When separated from this body, the soul is immediately in a state more &#8220;natural&#8221; to it, closer to the state God intends for it; for the resurrected &#8220;spiritual body&#8221; in which man will dwell in the Kingdom of Heaven has more in common with the soul than with the body we know on earth.</p></blockquote>
<h4>What will our resurrected body be like?</h4>
<blockquote><p>[The] resurrected body, like that of Christ Himself, will be different from our earthly bodies in that it will be more refined and more like the angelic nature, without which it could not dwell in the Heavenly Kingdom, where there is no death or corruption; but it will still be the same body, miraculously restored and made fit by God for eternal life, as Ezekiel saw in his vision of the &#8220;dry bones&#8221; (Ezek. 37:1-14).</p></blockquote>
<h4>Erroneous concepts of heaven</h4>
<blockquote><p>many Christians, in order to escape the mockery and unbelievers and avoid even the slightest taint of any materialistic conception, have gone to an opposite extreme and declare that heaven is &#8220;nowhere.&#8221; Among Roman Catholics and Protestants there are sophisticated apologies which proclaim that heaven is &#8220;a state, not a place,&#8221; that &#8220;up&#8221; is only a metaphor, the Ascension of Christ (Luke 24:50-51, Acts 1:9-11) was not really an &#8220;ascension,&#8221; but only a change of state. The result of such apologies is that heaven and hell become very vague and indefinite conceptions, and the sense of their reality begins to disappear&#8212;with disastrous results for Christian life, because these are the very realities toward which our whole earthly life is directed.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>The Christian after-death experiences all affirm the existence of heaven, hell, and judgment, of the need for repentance, struggle, and fear of losing one&#8217;s soul eternally; while the contemporary experiences, like those of shamans, pagan initiates, and mediums, seem to point to a &#8220;summerland&#8221; of pleasant experiences in the &#8220;other world,&#8221; where there is no judgment but only &#8220;growth,&#8221; and death is not to be feared but only welcome as a &#8220;friend&#8221; that introduces one to the pleasures of &#8220;life after death.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>What to do when someone you know dies</h4>
<blockquote><p>As soon as someone has reposed, immediately call or inform a priest, so he can read the &#8220;Prayers on the Departure of the Soul,&#8221; which are appointed to be read over all Orthodox Christians after death. Try, if it be possible to have the funeral in church and to have the Psalter read over the deceased until the funeral. The funeral need not be performed elaborately, but most definitely it should be complete, without abbreviations; think at this time not of yourself and your convenience, but of the deceased, with whom you are parting forever.</p></blockquote>
<h4>The spiritual world is merging with ours</h4>
<blockquote><p>St. Gregory the Dialogist: &#8220;As the present world approaches its end, the world of eternity looms nearer The end of the world merges with the beginning of eternal life The spiritual world is moving closer to us, manifesting itself through visions and revelations.&#8221; The end of this world&#8217;s existence began with the coming of Christ, and sensitive souls are always seeing how the other world is &#8220;breaking into&#8221; this world ahead of time and giving &#8220;hints&#8221; of its existence.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>The only way to heaven is through Lord Jesus Christ</h4>
<blockquote><p>The Church&#8217;s teaching is that whereas before our redemption by Christ, no one could pass through the air to heaven, the path being closed by demons, and all men went down to hell, now it has become possible for men to pass through the demons of the air, and their power now is restricted to men whose own sins convict them. In the same way, we know that even though Christ &#8220;destroyed the power of hell&#8221; (Kontakion of Pascha), any one of us can still fall into hell by rejecting salvation in Christ.</p></blockquote>
<p>I see the toll-houses as a way for God to show you his just judgment. It&#8217;s a fair court trial with detailed evidence presented by your accusers&#8212;the demons&#8212;and defended competently by the holy angels. Whoever ends up in hell after the Last Judgment will have no doubt why they are there, and has no standing to whine that God is unfair or arbitrary. With <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Soul-After-Death-Seraphim-Rose/dp/093863514X?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=cea994ebdb79104879501bacb34550a2&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">The Soul After Death</a>, Father Seraphim Rose did a commendable job revealing the doctrine of death and the importance of believing in the truth instead of vague modern notions that try to exalt death for everyone, regardless of what type of lives they had. (For a podcast adaption of the book, listen to Father John Valadez&#8217;s <a href="https://www.sttimothy.net/index.php/2021/01/20/the-soul-after-death-lecture-series/">Soul After Death lecture series</a>. For a more academic approach to this topic, try Jean-Claude Larchet&#8217;s <a href="https://www.amazon.com/after-Death-According-Orthodox-Tradition/dp/088465477X?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=ae260972e91142ead66f8e798abd2fc4&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">Life After Death</a>.)</p>
<p>One caveat is that, unless you are firmly on the path of Orthodoxy, you will feel notions of despair about the perceived difficulty of being saved, at least from the anecdotes that were shared involving mostly monks who were greatly tried at their final hour. I purposefully did not share any of the hard sayings since my audience is not solely Orthodox. I cannot recommend this book to those not in the Orthodox Church except for those who have had near-death or out-of-body experiences and have fallen into a &#8220;spiritual but not religious&#8221; trap that needs to be corrected. If you&#8217;re Orthodox, this is essential reading to understand the stakes at hand.</p>
<p><strong>Learn More:</strong> <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Soul-After-Death-Seraphim-Rose/dp/093863514X?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=cea994ebdb79104879501bacb34550a2&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl"><em><strong>The Soul After Death on Amazon</strong></em></a></p>

																<div class="entry-meta below-title">

						<img width="1060" height="594" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-1060x594.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-1060x594.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-300x168.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-1024x574.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-768x430.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-550x308.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-892x500.jpg 892w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail-600x336.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/10/thumbnail.jpg 1285w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>

													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>In this talk, which I gave on September 17 at <a href="https://tradforum.com/wp/">Trad Forum</a>, I share five common worldly attachments that I&#8217;ve been struggling with since becoming a Christian. I discuss my experiences with these attachments alongside advice from Orthodox Elders and Church Fathers. My hope with the talk is to help people identify all that may be competing with their love for God.</p>

																	<article id="post-15977" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-15977 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-faith category-orthodoxy">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/do-you-exempt-yourself-from-gods-law">Do You Exempt Yourself From God&#8217;s Law?</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/orthodoxy" rel="category tag">Orthodoxy</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/do-you-exempt-yourself-from-gods-law" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-09-26T10:00:00-04:00">
						September 26, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-09-23T18:36:19-04:00">
						September 23, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/do-you-exempt-yourself-from-gods-law#comments">14 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/do-you-exempt-yourself-from-gods-law">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-portrait-dark-hoodie-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>When a man begins repentance, his heart is tender, contrite, and humble. He is ready to follow God&#8217;s commandments, obey Church teachings, and begin a new life in Christ. The problem is he is not yet fully healed, and still has elevated pride that is automatic for those who grew up in the West. Very soon, he may begin to make exemptions for himself concerning various sins or practices that he rationalizes as &#8220;small,&#8221; &#8220;temporary,&#8221; or serving the &#8220;greater good.&#8221; Satan&#8217;s foot is back in the door and will use his desire for exemptions to launch a strong attack that steals away the seed of new faith.</p>
<p>In <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Crime-Punishment-Fyodor-Dostoyevsky/dp/0486415872?content-id=amzn1.sym.97762c05-7545-47e0-ae5c-1110ba2791f0%3Aamzn1.sym.97762c05-7545-47e0-ae5c-1110ba2791f0&amp;cv_ct_cx=crime+and+punishment&amp;keywords=crime+and+punishment&amp;pd_rd_i=0486415872&amp;pd_rd_r=b07a6451-1f3b-44c9-b101-f9f1a0176224&amp;pd_rd_w=uywmT&amp;pd_rd_wg=A9caU&amp;pf_rd_p=97762c05-7545-47e0-ae5c-1110ba2791f0&amp;pf_rd_r=ATN60XGVXDVWHJHN97DC&amp;qid=1663798559&amp;sr=1-3-965fba24-1eed-4536-936e-b447f98a83bc&amp;x=0&amp;y=0&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=2ee6eb68b893143a6e65f86493690e1c&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">Crime &amp; Punishment</a> by Fyodor Dostoevsky, the character Raskolnikov believes he is superior to his fellow man&#8212;so superior that he should have the right to kill someone if that person poses an obstacle to him.</p>
<blockquote><p>&#8220;I simply hinted that an extraordinary man has the right that is not an official right, but an inner right to decide in his own conscience to overstep certain obstacles, and only in case it is essential for the practical fulfilment of his idea (sometimes, perhaps, of benefit to the whole of humanity).&#8221;</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>There is, if you recollect, a suggestion that there are certain persons who can that is, not precisely are able to, but have a perfect right to commit breaches of morality and crimes, and that the law is not for them.</p></blockquote>
<p>Raskolnikov goes on to murder someone he thought was a detriment to mankind, and in the process of that murder he ended up killing a second person who happened upon the scene. By usurping the mantle of God, Raskolnikov thought that his intellectual powers gave him the ability to dispense with a perceived miscreant and scourge to society, but very soon he is overcome by a crushing guilt that he cannot silence.</p>
<p>Before my repentance, when I was living in Catholic Poland, I adhered to the concept of &#8220;cultural Christianity,&#8221; meaning that I saw the overall good that Christianity was doing to those who practiced the faith, but believed it was an &#8220;opiate for the masses,&#8221; a tool for merely average men and women who needed external rules to have peace in life instead of ravenously following their worldly desires and carnal passions. Since I thought I was an exalted man, bestowed with innumerable gifts, including intellectual, I was not required to follow Christian morality and could instead live without any limits to my behavior or actions. My feelings and will were supreme, just like Raskolnikov, and I created wholesale exemptions for myself to God&#8217;s law even though I saw moral benefit in it for mankind. I did not murder anyone physically, but by teaching sin so vigorously through my books and videos, I was an attempted murderer of the souls of men who used them to fornicate, and I aided in the corruption of women who had relations with me and the men who followed me. What peace did I have in this time? What calm entered my soul? I was <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/15-signs-youre-a-dopamine-slave">a dopamine junkie</a>, a slave to bodily pleasure, prone to anger, unstable in emotion, reeking of disgusting pride, and deluded into thinking that I could operate my mind and body in a way that was not intended by God. It took a family death to wake me up from my demonic delusion.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-15980" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-1024x679.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="471" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-1024x679.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-300x199.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-768x509.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-1536x1018.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-2048x1358.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-1060x703.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-550x365.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-754x500.jpg 754w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-1920x1273.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-1629x1080.jpg 1629w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/woman-party-temptation-dark-600x398.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>It&#8217;s common to meet unmarried Christian men who are in sexual relationships with women. They justify it by saying that they are &#8220;monogamous&#8221; and &#8220;will get married eventually,&#8221; but will such self-justification suffice upon Judgment Day? God&#8217;s law is clearly against fornication, adultery, and harlotry. No man is given a divine imperative to exempt himself. Do you really believe that God is pleased that you&#8217;re fornicating with &#8220;only&#8221; one woman at a time? From what I learned <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-is-orthodox-christianity">in the Orthodox Church</a>, such a man must stop fornicating until he gets married within the Church.</p>
<p>Even after I was received into the Church, I still made an exemption for myself that I can be the star of <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-end-of-roosh-hour">a popular live stream</a>, one that spiked my adrenaline and led to numerous sins stemming from pride. It took me months to follow the basic Church teaching of halting that which causes you to sin.</p>
<blockquote><p>True repentance is a change of the heart, and the change of evil ways into good ways. True repentance invariably creates shame and regret in the heart of the penitent, that he had acted so shamelessly and insubordinately toward God. There can be no true repentance when a man does not want to cease from sins and show obedience toward God. There is a delusional and false repentance, and therefore it is of no benefit to the penitent. For repentance and willful sinning are contrary things, and cannot exist together. &#8212;Saint Tikhon of Zadonsk in <a href="https://churchsupplies.jordanville.org/9780578235202/">On True Christianity Vol. 1</a></p></blockquote>
<p>God did not exempt me. I&#8217;m not exalted above others. I&#8217;m not a special boy. Without God, my natural gifts are more likely to be harnessed for evil than good. The morality we get from God is objective, clear, and for our eternal benefit; it&#8217;s our fallen weakness to shade it gray and think that God really wants us to transgress His law because we are somehow above it. Believing you can commit any type of sin to do a &#8220;favor&#8221; for God is delusion, and unfortunately, I am infected with it. What the Church teaches, I must abide, and if I ever get the notion that I don&#8217;t have to abide, I must conclude that a demon is whispering in my ear, and a damaging spiritual fall is near.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-salvation-of-your-soul-is-not-a-game"><em><strong>The Salvation Of Your Soul Is Not A Game</strong></em></a></p>
										</div> <!-- .entry-content -->
																			</article>
																	<article id="post-15964" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-15964 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-book-reviews category-faith category-orthodoxy">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/should-christians-study-the-book-of-acts">Should Christians Study The Book Of Acts?</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/book-reviews" rel="category tag">Book Reviews</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/orthodoxy" rel="category tag">Orthodoxy</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/should-christians-study-the-book-of-acts" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-09-19T10:00:09-04:00">
						September 19, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-09-14T18:25:30-04:00">
						September 14, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/should-christians-study-the-book-of-acts#comments">15 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/should-christians-study-the-book-of-acts">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/bible-light-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p><a href="https://www.amazon.com/Acts-Apostles-Commentary-Holy-Scriptures/dp/1942699158?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=c64d536929e14dc411577d2be48e58cd&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-14913" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/12/book-averky-acts.jpg" alt="" width="71" height="110" /></a></p>
<p>The Book of Acts continues where the Gospels left off and shows us how God further instructed the apostles through the Holy Spirit, the third person of the Trinity. It&#8217;s also important in documenting the early history of the Church. <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-struggle-for-virtue">Archbishop Averky</a>, former abbot of Holy Trinity Monastery in Jordanville, New York, offers a sound exegesis of the book in his volume <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Acts-Apostles-Commentary-Holy-Scriptures/dp/1942699158?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=c64d536929e14dc411577d2be48e58cd&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">The Acts of the Apostles</a>. My favorite passages are highlighted below.</p>
<h4>Why the book of Acts is so important</h4>
<blockquote><p>In this book, we see the fulfillment of those prophecies that the Lord uttered to His apostles in the Gospels. In it, we see the triumph of the faith of Christ over this fallen world, in spite of the human frailty of the apostles who had no money to ensure the success of their mission. In this book, we see how the apostles themselves became completely different people after the descent of the Holy Spirit. Fearlessly, with great self-rejection and courage, they preached the faith of Christ to the very end of the Greco-Roman civilized world, despite grievous persecutions. In a short time, they established many Christian communities who lived in the spirit of the commandments of the Gospels. The Book of Acts vividly shows us that the preaching of the Apostles was not the work of man, but of God</p></blockquote>
<h4>Being filled with the Holy Spirit on Pentecost</h4>
<blockquote><p>Even before [Pentecost] the apostles were given some spiritual gifts, but now they were filled with the Holy Spirit, for the fullness of gracious spiritual gifts now had descended upon them. They were transfigured, purified, sanctified, and enlightened by the action of the Spirit of God. It was as if they became completely different, new people, with the Holy Spirit as their constant inspiration and guide. The external manifestation of this grace-filled transfiguration was the speaking in tongues, something that Christ Himself foretold (Mark 16:17). As soon as this divine fire lit their souls, they began to praise and thank God in the natural exuberance of their holy ecstasy, glorifying the majesty of God.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>It was appropriate for the grace of the Spirit to be given on the same day as the giving of the ancient Law [Jewish Pentecost], because as the Saviour willed to commit Himself to His passion in no other time than the time of the killing of the lamb, in order to tie the truth with the prefiguration. Thus also the coming of the Spirit could not have been given at any other time than the day when the Law was given, in order to show that the Holy Spirit is the same Lawgiver of both the Old and the New Covenants In the same way that on Pentecost sheaves of the new fruits were gathered by many people from many different places to Jerusalem, so on this day it was appropriate that the first fruits of all nations living under heaven should gather into a single sheaf of piety, brought to God through the apostolic preaching.</p></blockquote>
<h4>The foreknowledge of God</h4>
<blockquote><p>It is important to note that [God&#8217;s] foreknowledge does not destroy human free will, for the predestination of God, expressed in prophecy, is founded only on His foreknowledge. God knows how a person will use his free will, and depending on this free choice, God predestines.</p></blockquote>
<h4>The gift of the Holy Spirit to Orthodox Christians</h4>
<blockquote><p>Before the coming of Christ, the greater part of mankind, the Gentiles, were deprived completely of the gifts of the Holy Spirit, while grace was given to some of the Jews who were chosen for a special ministry. In Christianity, every one of the faithful receives these gifts of grace through the sacraments.</p></blockquote>
<h4>The beginning of Christian worship</h4>
<blockquote><p>Every day, the Christian community participated in worship at the Temple of Jerusalem. Christianity was not a sect within Judaism, but rather, it was the completion and fulfillment of true Judaism. The entirety of the temple worship was established on the expectation of the Messiah, and so Christians could freely worship in the Second Temple. Because the Christians believed in a Messiah who had already come, their own unique worship would need time to develop in a form distinct from the worship of the Old Testament Judaism.</p>
<p>The beginning of such unique Christian worship was the establishment of the sacrament of the Eucharist, which in Acts is called the &#8220;breaking of bread.&#8221; To celebrate this mystery, the first Christians gathered in private homes&#8212;&#8220;from house to house&#8221;&#8212;where the Eucharist would be served in conjunction with the evening agape meal. The general character of these Christian gatherings is characterized by these words: &#8220;with gladness and simplicity of heart.&#8221; This is the fruit of living faith and the purity of a heart deeply involved in a burgeoning spiritual life, illumined by the abundant gifts of the Holy Spirit. Because of this, Christians were a model of true piety, even for the rest of the Jews who did not believe in Christ. Therefore, many respected them as &#8220;having favor with all the people.&#8221; This favorable reputation of Christians was the reason for the gradual increase in converts, an event that St Luke ascribes to the work of the Lord Himself: &#8220;and the Lord added to the church daily those who were being saved.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h4>Receiving help from God</h4>
<blockquote><p>The more severe the persecutions of the newly established Church, the more manifest is the miraculous help of God. By the command of the angel, immediately upon their release, the apostles fearlessly returned to preaching openly in the temple. This remarkable boldness and courage can be explained only by the grace of the Holy Spirit encouraging their natural strength, making them fearless.</p></blockquote>
<h4>The mistakes of Protestants</h4>
<blockquote><p>to the end of his days, [Apostle Paul] resolutely battled [the delusion that Christians must follow the Mosaic Law], and all his epistles are imbued with the thought that man is justified by faith in Christ, not by the works of the Law. This thought unfortunately has been perverted by the Protestants, who teach that good deeds are not necessary for salvation, even though Apostle Paul would never even think of maintaining such an idea. He insisted on the irrelevance of only the Mosaic Law for Christianity. &#8220;The works of the Law&#8221; refer only to the rites of the Law of Moses, not to good deeds in general.</p></blockquote>
<p>At only 120 pages, Archbishop Averky&#8217;s <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Acts-Apostles-Commentary-Holy-Scriptures/dp/1942699158?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=c64d536929e14dc411577d2be48e58cd&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">The Acts Of The Apostles</a> is a quick read that can be tackled alongside reading the Book of Acts. If you were edified by <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-best-exegesis-of-the-four-gospels">his Orthodox exegesis of the Gospels</a>, you will enjoy this book as well.</p>
<p><strong>Learn More:</strong> <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Acts-Apostles-Commentary-Holy-Scriptures/dp/1942699158?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=c64d536929e14dc411577d2be48e58cd&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl"><em><strong>The Acts Of The Apostles on Amazon</strong></em></a></p>
										</div> <!-- .entry-content -->
																			</article>
																	<article id="post-15949" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-15949 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-culture category-dating category-sex category-women">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/seduction-is-narcissism">Seduction Is Narcissism</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/culture" rel="category tag">Culture</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/dating" rel="category tag">Dating</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/sex" rel="category tag">Sex</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/women" rel="category tag">Women</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/seduction-is-narcissism" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-09-12T10:00:58-04:00">
						September 12, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-09-12T15:58:24-04:00">
						September 12, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/seduction-is-narcissism#comments">92 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/seduction-is-narcissism">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-seduction-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>Over the centuries, Christian courtship in the West has become distorted into seduction, and seduction into unbridled fornication, the &#8220;hookup culture&#8221; we have today. Seduction and romance were gateways to normalized sexual sin because they facilitated fallen man&#8217;s propensity to self-love through carnal pleasure. Adam and Eve&#8217;s innate desire to please and love God was transformed through the fall into a vulgar narcissism where we eagerly abuse and desecrate the bodies of others. To target someone and perform a set of behaviors in order for them to &#8220;like&#8221; you, and then harness those affections into sexual pleasure, is a side effect of demonic narcissism that is normalized in our time.</p>
<blockquote><p>Instead of pleasing God and instead of the humility and obedience to the Law of God and the Holy Church commanded by Christ, there now flourishes as never before truly diabolical pride: self-love, conceit, self-glorification, self-exaltation, vanity which oozes out of every pore, and seeking after popularity and earthly glory. This all leads naturally to hatred, envy, malice, and uncontrollable hostility, leading at times to frenzy, instead of to the mutual love and goodwill commanded by the Gospel&#8230; &#8212;Archbishop Averky in <a href="https://archbishopaverky.blogspot.com/2020/05/enemies-of-orthodoxy-in-modern-world.html">Enemies Of Orthodoxy In The Modern World</a></p></blockquote>
<p>Imagine what a modern woman does to attract a man she likes. She will wear tighter or more revealing clothing, put on lipstick to mimic the color of her lips during a state of arousal, stare deeply into his eyes as if he were the only reason for her existence, bite her lower lip, purposely allow her chest, hip, or shoulder to graze the man&#8217;s body, laugh purposefully at his jokes, feign interest in his hobbies, preen ceaselessly, apply chemical fragrances to her skin, and deliberately conceal her personal flaws. This is but a sample of the manipulative weapons a woman uses when she methodically targets a man&#8217;s lustful tendency to get him to desire her for sex or love.</p>
<p>Why does a woman do this? To feel the emotional pleasure of being desired, to be validated through a man&#8217;s attention, to create a narrative that displays social value to her friend group (i.e. brag), to alleviate boredom, and to fulfill her own physically lustful urges. Each of these reasons is for the self: <em>I want to feel good, I want to feel beautiful, I want to be desired, I want to experience physical ecstasy, I want to be loved, I want to be doted upon, I want to be happy, I want to be popular, I want to be in a relationship like my friends.</em> In such a seduction, the woman deceives herself into thinking that she likes the man, or even loves him, but in reality her behavior is a projection of her narcissism. She loves only herself, proven by the fact that there is no pure sacrifice or virtue displayed in the seduction&#8212;only the expectation of gain. If that gain is not forthcoming, she halts the seduction (often in anger) and moves on to another target who can elicit the desired outcome. She sees a man as a character in a play that she scripted to appeal to her imagination and long-held fantasies that developed since childhood from consuming thousands of hours of <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/why-do-you-consume-secular-content">secular entertainment and media</a>. In essence, seducing a man allows her to be the princess in her own movie, someone who a man would die for, the ultimate confirmation of her perceived self-worth.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-15953" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-date-bar-seduction-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>It&#8217;s similar when a man is seducing a woman. A man will claim he is fornicating for the physical benefits alone, but he is all too eager to share tales of his conquests, highlighting his need for emotional validation concerning his masculine prowess. Sadly, I fornicated with many women in my past not because I strongly desired them, but because I wanted to bond with other men by sharing all the details of the seduction and be rewarded with their commendation or laughter. If you were to ask the old me why I dived so wholeheartedly <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/8-personal-defects-that-allowed-me-to-worship-fornication-for-18-years">into carnal sin</a>, he would answer you thus: <em>I want to feel good, I want to feel masculine, I want to have fun, I want to show off to other men, I want to assert my superiority over others or get their attention, I want to be challenged, I want to think of myself as special or skilled, I want to be popular, I want to be the hero of my own movie.</em> It was all done for my pleasure and egotistical needs. The women were merely supporting characters in the play that I had written myself for myself. It was so easy to forget about them after a short time because they were a mere instrument of my own pride and self-love.</p>
<p>For women, seduction is a gourmet meal while for men it&#8217;s like a trip to McDonald&#8217;s. Men want something quick and easy that fills the belly without a long wait, which is why it&#8217;s so much more common for a man to &#8220;take one for the team&#8221; than a woman. A man is more likely to see hooking up with any woman as a replacement for masturbation instead of the potentially life-changing narrative that women may prescribe to it. In both cases, the world revolves around the seducer and what he or she wants. The degree of patience may vary, whereby women are usually more patient than men since their sexual urges are less acute, but both use the other to receive material benefits, whether to the ego or to the body, and any authentic love or generosity displayed is only done to continue receiving benefits, remaining always transactional without serving a higher purpose.</p>
<blockquote><p>All of the Holy Fathers, teaching on the spiritual life, with one voice agree that the root and source of all the passions is egoism or self-love, that is, unreasonable, wrongful love towards oneself. Egoism or self-love gives rise to three principal passions the three fundament roots of all the other passions: love of pleasure, greed, and love of glory. These three principal passions are enumerated in the Holy Scripture by the Apostle and Evangelist John the Theologian who says, Do not love the world or the things in the world For all that is in the world&#8212;the lust of the flesh, the lust of the eyes, and the pride of life&#8212;is not of the Father but is of the world (1 John 2:15-16). From these three principal passions in turn come the following eight passions: (1) gluttony, (2) fornication, (3) avarice, (4) anger, (5) sorrow, (6) despair, (7) vainglory, and (8) pride. These eight passions engender yet more and more passions which then branch out into a multitude of diverse and subtle variations of each of these principal passions. All of these innumerable passions tyrannize and torment the human heart, never giving a person rest and causing him unbearable suffering, from which he loses spiritual peace, inner balance, and tranquility of conscience. He feels deeply unhappy, sometimes experiencing truly hellish torment, as if experiencing the onset of those torments that inevitably await all unrepentant sinners &#8212;Archbishop Averky in <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-struggle-for-virtue">The Struggle For Virtue</a></p></blockquote>
<p>Let&#8217;s compare narcissistic seduction with Orthodox Christian courtship, where the <em>I</em> is removed and replaced with God. The self is no longer the main recipient of pleasure, happiness, or glory. Instead of a man using a woman as a vehicle for self-gratification, she is used as a vehicle to please God and serve His will for mankind. If a man identifies a woman he wants to marry, the questions on his mind will look entirely different compared to the narcissistic man: <em>Is this union pleasing to God? Is she the one that God wants me to marry? Is this union necessary to increase our faith and ultimately our salvation? What is the will of my Lord God?</em> Of course the woman must have some appealing traits, but the final decision to court her for marriage will depend not on personal satisfaction or pleasure but God&#8217;s good pleasure, which He can reveal to the man in time through a variety of methods. The me-centeredness of seduction is replaced with the God-centeredness of chaste courtship. The desire to receive pleasure is replaced by the desire to pick up a cross that pleases God and ultimately leads to salvation. Using a woman to receive bodily pleasure is replaced with loving a woman to receive divine pleasure (God&#8217;s grace).</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-15955" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/09/male-woman-wedding-orthodox-crowns-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>If you don&#8217;t possess the true faith of Orthodoxy, I deem it impossible to purely court for God instead of seduce for the self, even if you&#8217;re a &#8220;good person&#8221; and covet marriage for wholesome material goals. Subconsciously, you will seek out a woman who pleases you in the here and now, and since it&#8217;s typical that we attract a mate who is <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/you-attract-your-mirror-reflection">a mirror to our spiritual state</a>, you will attract a narcissist if you&#8217;re a narcissist. You will attract an egomaniac if you&#8217;re an egomaniac. You will attract a woman who is unconsciously serving Satan if you&#8217;re already serving Satan. On the other hand, if you&#8217;re a God-pleaser, you will attract a God-pleaser, for a God-hater will find it torturous to be with a God-pleaser. From this reality, it&#8217;s clear to see that the solution to finding the best spouse is to work on an Orthodox faith that is pleasing to God, but how many women instead devote their free time to makeup, clothing, or secular entertainment? How many men spend untold hours <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/4-reasons-why-lifting-in-gyms-is-a-bad-idea">building huge muscles</a> in a quest to spam a hundred women on Tinder after uploading shirt-less photos? Such behavior is surely a sign that more spiritual work must be done, because it&#8217;s only when we transcend the selfish needs of our flesh do we mature enough to enter a marriage with God at the helm.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/hugs-are-dangerous"><em><strong>Hugs Are Dangerous</strong></em></a></p>
