																	<article id="post-15934" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-15934 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-culture category-health category-lifestyle">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/are-viruses-actually-contagious">Are Viruses Actually Contagious?</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/culture" rel="category tag">Culture</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/health" rel="category tag">Health</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/lifestyle" rel="category tag">Lifestyle</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/are-viruses-actually-contagious" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-09-04T10:00:36-04:00">
						September 4, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-08-31T17:25:13-04:00">
						August 31, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/are-viruses-actually-contagious#comments">69 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/are-viruses-actually-contagious">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-2048x1365.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/woman-face-mask-virus-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p><a href="https://drtomcowan.com/products/breaking-the-spell-the-scientific-evidence-for-ending-the-covid-delusion?variant=41299699171481"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-15936" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/book-breakingthespell.jpg" alt="" width="75" height="110" /></a></p>
<p>The coronavirus pandemic has revealed to me that science is not what I believed it to be when I received a bachelor&#8217;s degree in microbiology in 2001. Instead of striving for the pure, unadulterated truth of the natural world, it has blatantly become an authoritarian vehicle to enslave and spiritually destroy human beings at the hands <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/bankers-rule-the-world">of oligarchs</a> who have the billions of dollars needed to fund science and therefore determine what is science. From my independent research into the germ theory of disease, which is the accepted theory of how we allegedly get sick from various pathogens, I can no longer say that I absolutely believe viruses are contagious.</p>
<p>A man who helped nudge me into my current belief is Dr. Tow Cowan, a medical doctor and researcher who has revealed the history of virology and other truths that were not taught to me in university. <a href="https://drtomcowan.com/products/breaking-the-spell-the-scientific-evidence-for-ending-the-covid-delusion?variant=41299699171481">Breaking The Spell</a> is a short 43-page book he wrote that reveals the sham of modern virology. After studying Dr. Cowan&#8217;s work and many others (see the reading list at the bottom of this article), I cannot in good conscience conclude that viruses are the main cause of respiratory illness and other diseases.</p>
<p><iframe loading="lazy" title="Contagion Myth -Session 1   Tom Cowan" width="710" height="399" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/T_soWxxZtCw?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>
<p>When I tell people that I don&#8217;t have a firm belief that viruses are contagious, they begin a series of &#8220;How about&#8230;&#8221; questions to which I sometimes have an answer and sometimes I don&#8217;t. If you&#8217;re new to virus skepticism, I hope the following passages from Dr. Cowan&#8217;s book and my explanations will be of aid.</p>
<h4>Epidemiological observations are not proof that viruses exist</h4>
<blockquote><p>For more than a hundred years, people observed that one sailor after another got sick on ships. Their teeth fell out, and many went into heart failure and died. For many, it was &#8220;obvious&#8221; that something was being passed&#8212;a contagion&#8212;from one sailor to the next. At some point, however, a sailor ate a lime; the whole thing went away because, in fact, the sick sailors were suffering from scurvy, a disease caused by vitamin C deficiency.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>There are many other examples illustrating how epidemiological observations have misled a medical profession stubbornly wedded to the idea of contagion. Beriberi and pellagra two well-known nutritional deficiencies, were considered for decades to be caused by a contagion. It turns out the case was B vitamin deficiency, which, as one would expect, would often show up in the same family members at the same time.</p></blockquote>
<p>Last year, I came down <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/a-foretaste-of-my-deathbed">with a flu-like illness</a> while traveling. I returned home and then three days later, my mother came down with a similar but milder illness. It seemed quite intuitive that something was transmitted from me to my mother, but in spite of the timing, I cannot say with proof that a virus was transmitted. I have the epidemiological observation that my mother got sick three days after me, but if I want to say a virus caused it, I would need to prove it. Scientists have not proven that a viral particle floating in the air can be the cause of illness once inhaled, ingested, or transmitted through blood. If I can&#8217;t say it&#8217;s a virus in the case of me and my mother then what happened? I don&#8217;t know, but just because I don&#8217;t know, I will not hop onto a deceptively intuitive theory that does not have sufficient evidential backing. (Another intuitive theory that many have fallen for is <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-theory-of-evolution-is-incompatible-with-christianity">evolution</a>.)</p>
<p>Do you believe in a yawn virus? Probably not, but I&#8217;m sure it has happened to you that someone you were with yawned, and then almost immediately after, you also yawned. We don&#8217;t attribute such yawn contagion to a particle. Do you believe in a haircut virus? When I see a man with a nice haircut, I look in the mirror and evaluate if I need a haircut as well, and sometimes I get one soon after. Since it is theorized that diseases are the body&#8217;s method of expelling toxins, it could be that when you see someone who is sick, your body does an evaluation if it should also expel toxins. There are many other theories available that are beyond the scope of this introductory article, and I cannot claim to know the complete answer, but I have not seen credible evidence that virus particles are the cause of flu-like disease or otherwise.</p>
<p>During the Spanish influenza, Milton Rosenau was tasked with researching exactly how it was infecting humans. After a series of experiments, he was unable to infect <em>anyone</em> with the alleged virus (then called Pfeiffer&#8217;s bacillus). He went so far as getting sick people to cough and exchange fluids with healthy volunteers, and when that didn&#8217;t work, he took fluid from dead people&#8217;s lungs and tried to use that to infect people. It still didn&#8217;t infect anyone!</p>
<blockquote><p>As the preliminary trials proved negative, we became bolder, and selecting nineteen of our volunteers, gave each one of them a very large quantity of a mixture of thirteen different strains of the Pfeiffer bacillus, some of them obtained recently from the lungs at necropsy; others were subcultures of varying age, and each of the thirteen had, of course, a different history. Suspensions of these organisms were sprayed with an atomizer into the nose and into the eyes, and back into the throat, while the volunteers were breathing in. We used some billions of these organisms, according to our estimated counts, on each one of the volunteers, but none of them took sick. <a href="https://viroliegy.com/2021/10/03/the-infectious-myth-busted-part-1-the-rosenau-spanish-flu-experiments-1918/">The Infectious Myth Busted: The Rosenau Spanish Flu Experiments</a></p></blockquote>
<p>I know this may be hard for you to believe, since you were bombarded with viral theory when you are a child, and everyone you know believes in it, but <em>they have never proved that viral diseases are caused by viruses</em>. It&#8217;s just an intuitive theory that has been accepted as fact. When <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/babylon-road-9-rocky-mountains-hanging-lake-salt-lake-city">I go to national parks in the United States</a>, there are information placards that say a particular rock formation is billions of years old. That is presented confidently as fact, but it is also a mere theory (Orthodox Church doctrine puts <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-old-is-the-earth">the age of the earth</a> at about 7000 years).</p>
<h4>How are viruses &#8220;isolated&#8221;? (Hint: they&#8217;re not)</h4>
<blockquote><p>In the history of medicine, not one published study shows the isolation of identical particles that would represent a disease-causing virus from any bodily fluid from any sick person.</p>
<p>Let me make this even more clear. If one takes any person with any &#8220;viral&#8221; illness&#8212;for example, chicken pox, rabies, measles, AIDS or COVID-19&#8212;the published literature does not contain any evidence of any virus that was directly isolated from any bodily fluids from even one person suffering from these illnesses. The interesting thing about this statement is that no health institution from any government in the world disagrees.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>&#8230;here are the steps Enders [the first scientist who &#8220;isolated&#8221; viruses&#8221;] outlined in his 1954 paper [describing viral isolation]. Enders started his experiment by taking a throat swab from seven children hospitalized with symptoms consistent with measles. He mixed the cotton swab with two milliliters of milk&#8212;interestingly, itself a source of genetic material. Then he added the throat swab in milk to a solution containing: &#8220;Penicillin, 100ug/ml and streptomycin, 50 mg/ml were added to all throat specimens which were then centrifuged at 5450 rpm for about one hour. Supernatant fluid and sediment resuspended in a small volume of milk were used as separate inocula in different experiments in amounts varying from 0.5 ml to 3.0 ml&#8221;.</p>
<p>&#8220;Inocula&#8221; is just the sample used in the next step, which was to inoculate this material onto a culture of &#8220;trypsinized human and rhesus monkey kidney&#8221; cells. To this culture medium, he added the following: &#8220;The culture medium consisted of bovine amniotic fluid (90%), beef embryo extract (5%), horse serum (5%), antibiotics, and phenol red as an indicator of cell metabolism&#8221;.</p>
<p>In simple language, Enders mixed his sample with six other substances that are known to be sources of protein and genetic material. We now know that these substances break down into particles with the size and morphology of what are called viruses. These six sources are milk, human kidney cells, rhesus monkey kidney cells, bovine amniotic fluid, beef embryo extract and horse serum.</p>
<p>To this culture, Enders&#8217; research group next added antibiotics that are known to be toxic to the kidney cells, especially streptomycin. (Nowadays, scientists tend to use the antibiotics gentamicin and amphotericin.) Enders and colleagues then observed this brew over a number of days. When they saw a characteristic cytopathic effect (CPE) in the cells of the cultures&#8212;meaning the transition of healthy, normal-sized culture cells into giant, disorganized cells with internal holes or vacuoles&#8212;they concluded that these were proof that the virus from the throat swab was destroying the cells in the culture. To Enders, this cytopathic effect was the hallmark of dying cells, and he believed it could only have occurred because the virus in the measles sample infected and destroyed the cells in the culture.</p>
<p>To this day, with minor exceptions, every &#8220;viral isolation&#8221; starts with this flawed culturing process. Furthermore, every genetic analysis of any purported virus is done on the results of this cell culture, not on an isolated, purified virus. No exceptions. Thus, if virologists want to elucidate the genome of a new virus, they don&#8217;t isolate the virus from a sick person and sequence that specific particle. Rather, they take an unpurified sample from a sick person, run it through a tissue culture (as described above) and do their analysis on the resulting mixture&#8212;not on the virus itself.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>every &#8220;live-viral vaccine&#8221; basically is nothing more than a partly purified (minimally filtered) cell culture mixture.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Today, virologists refer to the inevitable breakdown products of dead and dying tissues as extracellular vesicles or sometimes as &#8220;exosomes.&#8221; These particles can be isolated and purified directly from bodily fluids of sick people. They are conceptually different from viruses in that viruses supposedly come from outside the person and, at least sometimes, are considered pathogens. EVs come from the breakdown of the person&#8217;s own tissues and are non-pathogenic. And, as of May 2020, virologists acknowledged that they can&#8217;t distinguish between the two. There is only one realistic explanation for this. All particles with the size, composition and morphology of &#8220;viruses&#8221; are, in reality, the normal and inevitable results of the breakdown of our own tissues. And our tissues break down for the same reason as the cultures in Enders&#8217; experiments broke down: They&#8217;re either starved, poisoned or both. Dying tissues produce a myriad of particles, and these particles have unfortunately been mistaken for pathogenic, exogenous viruses. It&#8217;s time to clear up this misconception.</p></blockquote>
<p>If I hand you a canister and tell you it&#8217;s gasoline, you will assume that the liquid inside is only gasoline. If I give you a bottle of extra virgin olive oil, you will assume it only has extra virgin olive oil without adulterants. With virus isolation, however, you&#8217;re getting a potpourri of genetic and medicinal junk in addition to the alleged virus. A virus &#8220;isolate&#8221; is anything but. They have not isolated any viruses, so whenever you hear in the news that a new virus has been isolated, they are using a definition of isolation that is quite different than what you would expect by the word &#8220;isolation.&#8221; To help convince you of their sham, they will say they&#8217;ve used electron microscopes and various dyes, pointing with a soy meme expression that the little particles are viruses that will go on to infect other human beings, when really it&#8217;s just cell junk and debris that is created when you expose healthy mammalian cells of various animals to a toxic brew.</p>
<h4>Coronavirus spike proteins are only seen after adding protein-digesting enzymes</h4>
<blockquote><p>The authors [in a paper announcing the discover of coronavirus spike proteins] then describe the electron micrographs done on the resulting culture fluid: &#8220;Electron micrographs of sectioned Vero/hSLAM cells showed cytoplasmic membrane-bound vesicles containing coronavirus particles. Following several failures to recover virions with the characteristic fringe of surface spike proteins, it was found that adding trypsin to the cell culture medium immediately improved virion morphology.&#8221;</p>
<p>In other words, the particles the Australian researchers call &#8220;coronaviruses&#8221; included the characteristic halo of spike proteins only after the investigators added trypsin to the culture medium. Trypsin is a protein-digesting enzyme; viruses are alleged to have a protein &#8220;coat.&#8221; It would be reasonable to assume that if one adds protein-digesting enzymes to particles with a protein coating, some of the protein coating will be eaten away, leaving a final particle that might look in an electron micrograph as if it has spikes. This lab-induced result obviously would bear no relationship to what such a particle might look like inside a live person.</p>
<p>There is only one rational, logical and scientific conclusion that one can draw from this paper: These researchers had no idea what made the Vero/hSLAM cells break down. Moreover, they had no idea where any genetic material they subsequently tested for originated. Finally, they did not find any particle with the characteristic morphology of a coronavirus until they manufactured its appearance. In sum, there is no evidence in this paper that any particle known as SARS-CoV-2 was found, or that any virus had anything to do with this Australian person&#8217;s illness.</p></blockquote>
<p>Spike proteins are a laboratory-made creation. They have not been observed in human tissue nor isolated from them. They do not exist naturally. If you&#8217;re watching a video of a based scientist who is telling you the &#8220;truth&#8221; of spike proteins as compared to establishment scientists, he is also far from the truth, despite his good intentions. Starting in the year 2020, there has been a wave of illnesses around the world, but I do not believe it is caused by coronavirus or spike proteins, and any research or content that discusses these alleged particles as the cause of illness is probably a waste of your time.</p>
<h4>The coronavirus PCR test is actually a test for common human, bacterial, and fungal DNA</h4>
<blockquote><p>Doing a BLAST search for the Drosten primer sequences [of SARS-CoV-2], Davis came up with more than 90 matching sequences in the human genome and more than 90 matching sequences in the microbial world. This finding means that the primer sequences being used in RT-PCR testing to identify &#8220;SARS-CoV-2&#8221; could be possibly of human or microbial (bacterial, fungal, etc.) origin. Any claims that these PCR primer sequences are unique to SARS-CoV-2 are, therefore, false.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>all illness creates genetic debris, and similar illnesses cause similar patterns of genetic breakdown. When these patterns are picked up by the PCR process and erroneously used as a diagnostic test, that is when we run into trouble.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>The biggest danger of using the PCR process as a diagnostic test is that the number of cycles will determine the percentage of positives and negatives. Any PCR &#8220;test&#8221; done with 25 or fewer cycles is likely to be negative in almost every case. With that amount of amplification, one rarely is able to pick up the primer sequence in question. On the other hand, if the amplification cycles are above 40, almost everyone will test positive because those sequences are present in every human-and every human has a baseline of tissue breakdown happening all the time.</p>
<p>The implications of this feature of the PCR process are clear. If any tyrant wanted to show that there was a &#8220;viral pandemic,&#8221; all they would have to do is increase the cycle numbers to more than 40. If they then wanted to show that whatever intervention they were using to combat this &#8220;pandemic&#8221; was helping, they could just lower the cycles to fewer than 25. Suddenly, all those &#8220;positive&#8221; cases would become &#8220;negative&#8221; simply because the sensitivity of the test was altered.</p>
<p>The only way to combat this potential fraud is to eliminate the use of any PCR process as a diagnostic test.</p></blockquote>
<p>Most people I know have fallen for the &#8220;coronavirus is infectious&#8221; sham and relay their adventures with clinical testing. Today they test negative, and three days later they still test negative, and then a day after that they test positive. From my observation, those who don&#8217;t have symptoms seem more likely to test positive. Coronavirus testing is a spin of the roulette wheel because it does not test for what it claims to test. Instead of testing for a virus, it&#8217;s actually testing for burrowed pieces of your own DNA that sometimes shows up on the test. The result it generates could be completely random.</p>
<p>Dr. Cowan&#8217;s explanation of the virus sham is thorough, logical, elegant, and clear, because instead of merely theorizing, he&#8217;s deconstructing the research papers from the virologists themselves who have made claims that later became normalized in <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/western-medicine-is-dead">medical science</a>. He&#8217;s using the words and techniques of the scientists to show how ridiculous their research and &#8220;isolation&#8221; really is. This means that the viral model for disease is a theory, just like the theory of evolution, and we already know how wrong that theory is. Scientists have not isolated viruses and have not proved they cause disease unlike with bacteria or parasites. Something is being communicated when you get sick after spending time with someone else who is sick, but there is absolutely no proof that it&#8217;s a virus.</p>
<p>After Dr. Cowan debunks modern medicine, he then theorizes about what he believes is really going on. This is where he loses me. In the last chapter of his book, he proposes a theory of water crystallization that ends up deifying water and how it can rearrange itself ad-hoc into needed biochemical structures. He stresses this is just a theory, but it&#8217;s one I do not accept. I did discover that Dr. Cowan believes in a spiritual reality, which is more than most modern scientists who are pompously atheist. I find that scientists who at least believe in God are more likely to be closer to the truth of our material world.</p>
<p>Scientists in the 20th century were sure that certain diseases were spreading from person to person, but they were being caused by something other than bacteria, parasites, or fungi. So what did they do? They invented a particle called the virus to solve the problem. All the scientists who believed in emerging viral theory went on to receive much acclaim, prestige, and financial success as many billions of research dollars poured into an exciting new field that was extremely profitable to pharmaceutical companies developing vaccines, which are essentially soups of cell culture mixed with toxic preservatives. Lies seem to have a momentum of their own, and viruses are just one of many lies that the average secular person believes in. (Ironically, I think that scientists may have created or become close to creating a man-made virus, or at least harmful biological matter that has a greater ability to spread than purely chemical agents.)</p>
<p>So what&#8217;s causing illness? I don&#8217;t know, but I do have my suspicions about <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/stop-eating-seed-oils-challenge">seed oils</a>, environmental toxins, and electromagnetic waves. The fascinating and well-researched book <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Invisible-Rainbow-History-Electricity-Life-ebook/dp/B084SZW2LC?keywords=invisible+rainbow&amp;qid=1661878726&amp;sr=8-1&amp;x=0&amp;y=0&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=1c2dbd908616d22730547b3cbfe21d41&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">The Invisible Rainbow</a> makes a very strong case that every stepwise advancement in radio and telecommunications technology has resulted in a worldwide &#8220;pandemic.&#8221; Getting sick from electromagnetic waves would end up having a similar epidemiology to person-to-person transmission. How else can we explain why sailors far at sea would get sick with flu-like illnesses at the same time as those on land?</p>
<blockquote><p>If influenza is primarily an electrical disease, a response to an electrical disturbance of the atmosphere, then it is not contagious in the ordinary sense. The patterns of its epidemics should prove this, and they do.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>The English warship Arachne was cruising off the coast of Cuba without any contact with land. No less than 114 men out of a crew of 149 fell ill with influenza and only later was it learnt that there had been outbreaks in Cuba at the same time.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>During the 19181919 pandemic, monkeys and baboons perished in great numbers in South Africa and Madagascar, sheep in northwest England, horses in France, moose in northern Canada, and buffalo in Yellowstone.47 There is no mystery here. We are not catching the flu from animals, nor they from us. If influenza is caused by abnormal electromagnetic conditions in the atmosphere, then it affects all living things at the same time, including living things that dont share the same viruses or live closely with one another. &#8212;The Invisible Rainbow</p></blockquote>
<p>If this is your first exposure to the &#8220;viruses aren&#8217;t contagious&#8221; position, I&#8217;m sure you&#8217;re skeptical and filled with questions, because I sure was. This article is not meant to be exhaustive, and cannot possibly answer all of your &#8220;what ifs&#8221; and &#8220;how abouts,&#8221; but as a truth-seeker, where truth is all that is from God, I can no longer believe in modern viral theory without question. The theory does seem intuitive at first glance from our own epidemiological experiences, but the facts don&#8217;t support the existence of a transmissible virus. I need to see direct, causative proof and not mere correlation or conjecture.</p>
<p>Unfortunately, we don&#8217;t have the absolute truth of why we get various illnesses, and while industrial food and EMF radiation are strong contenders as causes, it seems that God does not want us to know everything about disease and illness, and He is using them as part of His plan to save the souls of men. People of old never thought that diseases were caused by particles but instead were the result of God&#8217;s will; perhaps that is where we must return. I don&#8217;t believe in the scientists, but I do believe in God, so whatever the cause of the next disease I have, may His will be done.</p>

													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>The &#8220;hangry&#8221; meme is real. If you don&#8217;t eat for a while, you are more susceptible to the negative states of anger and irritation than if you were sated. This poses a problem for Orthodox Christians, who fast from animal products for about half the calendar year, not only abstaining from certain types of food but also reducing overall portion sizes. How can we perform the fast without falling into grumpiness that may open the door to passionate sins?</p>
<blockquote><p>Can anyone think that where there is no prayer and fasting, the devil is already there? One can! &#8212;Saint Theophan the Recluse</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>Anyone who rejects the effort of prayer and fasting is capable of doing nothing but evil&#8212;and all his apparent good, if he has any, is in truth not good at all, but also evil; because according to Christ&#8217;s words: &#8220;A corrupt tree cannot bring forth good fruit&#8221;: &#8220;do men gather grapes from thorns or figs from thistles?&#8221; (Matt. 7:18,16). &#8220;Beware,&#8221; Christ therefore says, &#8220;of false prophets which come to you in sheep&#8217;s clothing, but inwardly they are ravening wolves&#8221; (Matt. 7:15). &#8212;<a href="https://archbishopaverky.blogspot.com/2019/02/bearing-cross.html">Archbishop Averky</a></p></blockquote>
<p>The key to understanding your mood in a state of hunger is blood glucose. After you eat a meal that contains glucose, which is found in sugars and carbohydrates, your body shuttles that glucose to your muscles and brain, where it is used as an immediate and accessible energy source. For the glucose that is not immediately utilized, your body converts it to glycogen. As an analogy, we can liken glycogen to glucose stored in a closed bottle and put on the shelf (it&#8217;s actually multiple glucose molecules chained together).</p>
<p>Depending on your unique physiology, your blood glucose concentration will dip 2-3 hours after eating. Your brain and muscles continually need glucose, so through a complex mechanism called glycogenolysis, the &#8220;bottle of glucose&#8221; (glycogen) is retrieved from the shelf and opened to release the amount of glucose that is needed for you to function normally.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-15921" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-1024x765.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="530" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-1024x765.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-300x224.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-768x574.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-1536x1147.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-1060x792.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-550x411.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-669x500.jpg 669w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-1446x1080.jpg 1446w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose-600x448.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/blood-glucose.jpg 1600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>The amount of glycogen stored in your body is not unlimited: you have about 2,000 calories worth stored in your muscles and liver. If you&#8217;re an athlete and hit the &#8220;wall&#8221; during intense activity, unable to perform further, you have <a href="https://8fit.com/fitness/glycogen-depletion-signs-symptoms-and-working-out/">used up all of your glycogen</a> (and free glucose). You have run out of gas, so to speak, but you do not need to be an athlete to run out of preferred energy stores. It is estimated that a sedentary person who is fasting from food will extinguish all their glycogen in 12-22 hours, and that will depend on their muscular physique, metabolism, and general level of activity.</p>
<p>If you run out of glycogen and do not have an immediate food source, do you soon die? No, our all-wise God has implanted an exceedingly complex mechanism in the animal world called gluconeogenesis which converts fat into glucose. What&#8217;s amazing about the gluconeogenesis pathway is that fats contain no glucose molecules at all, but God has easily found a way to make the chemistry work. Gluconeogenesis will occur during prolonged exercise and fasting, or if you&#8217;re eating a low-carb diet. There&#8217;s only one major issue with gluconeogenesis: it&#8217;s slow.</p>
<p>Your body can convert glycogen to glucose pretty fast, but converting fats to glucose takes more time and happens in a stepwise fashion like a home thermostat slowly arriving at a set temperature. Therefore, if you&#8217;re all out of glycogen, you will enter a state where your body does not have a preferred energy source. During that time, you will begin to feel the classic symptoms of fatigue, mood irritation (i.e. &#8220;hangry&#8221;), bodily weakness, and even pain in the form of headaches.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-13684" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-1024x702.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="487" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-1024x702.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-300x206.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-768x527.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-1536x1053.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-2048x1405.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-1060x727.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-550x377.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-729x500.jpg 729w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-1920x1317.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-1575x1080.jpg 1575w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/big-brain-600x411.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>When I&#8217;m hungry, and have not eaten for over 12 hours, I often enter a state of irritation. I&#8217;m much <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-psychology-of-complaining">more likely to complain</a> and snap at those who are close to me for the most trivial of reasons. I&#8217;ve since learned to <em>not talk at all</em> when I&#8217;m hungry, at risk of saying something I regret. Spiritually, I was told by a monk that not eating reveals the naked state of your being when it&#8217;s not being sated with food or some other pleasure. I have a history of anger and irritation, so when I&#8217;m not being fed, those problems are able to directly rise to the surface. Modern scientists theorize (i.e. guess) that glucose is needed to control the willpower centers of the brain. When your brain doesn&#8217;t have glucose, they say, it shuts down the willpower to be a decent human being.</p>
<p>I would have believed the biological theory if I wasn&#8217;t an <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-is-orthodox-christianity">Orthodox Christian</a>, where states of grace can transcend the body&#8217;s immediate biological needs. This year, I went to a monastery for the first week of Lent. For several days in a row, I was able to eat the one served meal a day, something I had never done before, and experienced no irritation or anger. I didn&#8217;t even feel weak. The reason is I was attending several hours a day of services. My soul was able to use any grace received from the services to supplant my body&#8217;s need for food, but then the grace ended and I could not stop thinking of food. I again felt the desire to eat multiple times a day along with sharp periods of irritation.</p>
<p>There is certainly a biological reality, for we do exist in the body, but it does not supplant the spiritual reality of grace that God gives to our soul at His discretion. An Orthodox Christian only needs to read the lives of the saints to see countless examples of men eating only bread and salt for prolonged periods. It&#8217;s not that these saints were anatomical supermen like professional athletes, but they so pleased God that their faith was able to suspend biological laws by grace for a sustained period.</p>
<p>When I&#8217;m at home and only attending one or two divine services a week, I don&#8217;t have much in the way fasting grace, and every day is a struggle. I&#8217;m tempted to eat three meals a day or else I&#8217;m grumpy and can&#8217;t take my mind off food. From these struggles, here are five things I&#8217;ve learned on my quest to fast better&#8230;</p>
<p><strong>1. If I&#8217;m getting angry and cannot control my thoughts or speech, it&#8217;s better to eat.</strong> Our faith is a faith of love, so if you&#8217;re a heroic faster but you&#8217;re having angry thoughts or actually attacking those close to you, you may be missing the point of the fast.</p>
<p><strong>2. It takes about 30-120 minutes for your mood to be restored after eating. </strong>The bigger the meal you eat, the longer it will take for your body to digest the glucose. For an acute attack, you can try eating a couple tablespoons of honey with a slice of bread for faster relief.</p>
<p><strong>3. It&#8217;s easier to fast for yourself than to fast for God.</strong> Before I came to Christ, I often did intermittent fasting and regularly went for 18 hours without eating. The reason I fasted was to improve my appearance to aid in achieving sin with women. Satan helped me every step of the way, and I did not notice being grumpy or having angry thoughts, probably because I liked my passions and thought it was an irrevocable part of <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/who-are-you">my identity</a>. To do the Orthodox fast is significantly harder because there is no worldly gain from it and the standard of Christian love is quite high.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-15924" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/brunch-breakfast-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p><strong>4. Moderate bodybuilding can make you ravenously hungry.</strong> If I don&#8217;t do any workouts, and sit in front of my computer all day, I can eat two medium-sized meals without too many tears, but if I just do a little callisthenic training, I become rather hungry on the day of the exercise and the day after, and when I do eat, I have to fight the temptation to eat big. For fasting periods like Lent, you may want to <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/4-reasons-why-lifting-in-gyms-is-a-bad-idea">tone down your workouts</a> so that your fasting is not unnecessary hard.</p>
<p><strong>5. Don&#8217;t immediately run to the pantry upon the first hunger pain.</strong> You won&#8217;t starve, though you may be tempted to believe so. I wait an hour for the sharp hunger pain to morph more into a dull ache.</p>
<blockquote><p>This is the mark of Christianity: however much a man toils and however many righteous acts he performs; he must feel that he has done nothing. In fasting he must say, &#8220;This is not fasting,&#8221; and in praying, &#8220;I have not prayed,&#8221; and in perseverance at prayer, &#8220;I have shown no perseverance; I am only just beginning to practice asceticism and to take pains.&#8221; And even if he is righteous before God, he should say, &#8220;I am not righteous, not I; I do not struggle, but barely make a beginning each day.&#8221; &#8212;Saint Makarios of Egypt in <a href="https://stanthonysmonastery.org/products/the-fifty-spiritual-homilies">The Fifty Spiritual Homilies</a></p></blockquote>
<p>I&#8217;m a mediocre faster at best. I can abide by the dietary restrictions without much anguish, but I still eat a good amount and do not always lose weight during prolonged fasts. In times of grace where my prayer is strong and I&#8217;m attending daily services, I can fast harder, but while at home I am able to only do the bare minimum. Thankfully, God does grade us based on effort and struggle instead of pounds lost. With the knowledge of how my body works, and the fact that fasting separates me from the world to draw nearer to God, I continue to fast, and hope that my fasting becomes stronger in the years to come.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/how-coffee-alcohol-addictions-are-linked"><em><strong>How Coffee &amp; Alcohol Addictions Are Linked</strong></em></a></p>
										</div> <!-- .entry-content -->
																			</article>
																	<article id="post-15909" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-15909 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-faith category-life">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/who-are-you">Who Are You?</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/life" rel="category tag">Life</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/who-are-you" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-08-22T10:00:33-04:00">
						August 22, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-08-17T12:22:05-04:00">
						August 17, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/who-are-you#comments">24 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/who-are-you">
						<img width="1060" height="707" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-1060x707.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-2048x1366.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-1920x1280.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-woman-mirror-date-600x400.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>Sometimes I wonder what is the most essential ingredient that makes me, me. Over the years I had many ideas of who I was, but it turned out that I was none of those things. And then I was absolutely sure I was other things, more internal things, but I was not those either, and the question remained unanswered.</p>
<p>In university, I thought I was my grades. If I got good grades, I was told, I would get a high-paying job and eventually be happy. If my grades were higher than my peers, I felt smarter than them, and if my grades were lower, I felt dumber. In the end, when my schooling was completed and I began to live a <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/secular-success-vs-christian-success">standard secular life</a>, I discovered that I was not my grades.</p>
<p>As an adult, away from my parent&#8217;s nest, I thought I was my income, my car, my possessions. I thought what I owned would define me and differentiate me. If my income was higher than others, I was more successful than them, a better person, and if it was lower, I was inferior. My stuff had to be better than other people&#8217;s stuff, but in the end, I discovered that I was not the items I own or what is in my bank account.</p>
<p>Then I fell for the idea that I was my experiences, particularly my travel experiences and relations with women. The countries I visited would define me; the women I fell with would make up my identity. I was a traveler, a &#8220;player.&#8221; If I had traveled to more countries or slept with more women than you, I thought I was superior to you, but in the end, I discovered I was nothing external to me, nothing that could be grasped in this material world.</p>
<blockquote><p>When someone is empty of Christ then a thousand and one other things come to fill his soul: jealousies, hatreds, boredom, melancholy, negativity, a worldly frame of mind and worldly pleasures. Try to fill your soul with Christ so as not to have it empty. Your soul is like a cistern full of water. If you channel the water to the flowers, that is, to the virtues, you will experience true joy and all the thorns of evil will wither away. But if you channel the water to the weeds, these will grow and choke you and all the flowers will wither. &#8212;Saint Porphyrios in <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/learning-to-love-god">Wounded By Love</a></p></blockquote>
<p>So I must be my personality. I am my sense of humor, my quirks, my demeanor, my attitude. I am all the things that cannot be precisely duplicated in anyone else. If I made more people laugh than you, I had a better personality. If more people wanted to hear what I had to say, I was more interesting. I cannot so easily say that my personality is not me, because if it is not me then what is me? But then I asked, where exactly does my humor come from? Does it really come from inside me or was it influenced over the years by factors outside of me and by the milieu I live in? Does not my quirks, demeanor, and attitude, come mostly from my parents and upbringing? Doesn&#8217;t the way I act come mostly from wanting to become some kind of ideal of a man as defined by the culture? In the end, I had to conclude that I was not exactly my personality, which to my surprise has changed in major ways over the past few years <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/gods-revelation-to-the-human-heart">through God&#8217;s grace</a>.</p>
<p>I got it: I must be my thoughts. Many people have told me that I&#8217;m &#8220;sharp&#8221; and &#8220;intelligent,&#8221; and this must be because of the way my brain works on a functional, biological level. It is unique and solely mine, irreplaceable and unchangeable. My thoughts are definitely me&#8230; until they come <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/demons-can-put-thoughts-into-your-mind">from the demons</a> in the form of judgments, temptations, and vulgarities. Or until they come from God or His angels in the inspiration to do a good deed. How can my thoughts be &#8220;me&#8221; if they can derive from beings external to me, if I can serve as a vessel for unseen spiritual forces? In fact, I cannot even prove to you that the words written here are definitively from me and me alone. In the end, I concluded that my thoughts are not solely me, and neither is anything else that allows me to compare myself with others in any way.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-15914" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-1024x683.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="474" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-1024x683.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-768x512.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-1536x1024.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-1060x707.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-550x367.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-750x500.jpg 750w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-1620x1080.jpg 1620w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers-600x400.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/08/male-sleeping-flowers.jpg 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>There is not much else I can declare as being me. It can&#8217;t be my body, which is constantly changing and will soon not be mine when I die. It can&#8217;t be my relationships with other people, which are also changing by the day. It&#8217;s not the foods I eat, the way I pray, or even <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-salvation-of-your-soul-is-not-a-game">my favorite books</a>. No, those are all external; they aren&#8217;t me. So who am I? There is something in me that is &#8220;me&#8221; but I can&#8217;t grasp it with my hands or my mind.</p>
<p>One evening, in a state of contemplation, I looked up at one of my icons of Lord Jesus Christ. I asked Him, &#8220;Lord, who am I?&#8221; I stared at the icon for some time and then I felt a warmth in my heart, and the thought that came to me was, &#8220;You are a creature of God who can perceive God and give glory to Him, and behold His beauty with indescribable joy for all eternity.&#8221; And that thought seemed correct to me, that the &#8220;I&#8221; in I is a soul, a spiritual vessel, to recognize the God of all creation, the only faculty which makes me me, which will stay with me forever, and that I can only be defined according to my relationship with my Creator, and all that is separate or apart from my relationship with God is not me, and will soon pass away, and how eagerly do I await the day that I can commune in divine fullness, clarity, and love with the Father, the Son, and Holy Spirit, unto the ages of ages.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/i-lived-most-of-my-life-under-demonic-influence"><em><strong>I Lived Most Of My Life Under Demonic Influence</strong></em></a></p>
										</div> <!-- .entry-content -->
																			</article>
																	<article id="post-15786" class="is-cat-link-border-bottom post-15786 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-culture category-faith category-life category-orthodoxy">
										<header class="entry-header">
																						<h2 class="entry-title">
												<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/an-orthodox-examination-of-my-foolish-psychedelic-experience">An Orthodox Examination Of My Foolish Psychedelic Experience</a>
											</h2>
																<div class="entry-meta below-title">
									<span class="cat-links">
				<span class="prefix">
					in				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/culture" rel="category tag">Culture</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/faith" rel="category tag">Faith</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/life" rel="category tag">Life</a> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/category/orthodoxy" rel="category tag">Orthodoxy</a>			</span>
					<span class="posted-on">
				<span class="prefix">
					on				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/an-orthodox-examination-of-my-foolish-psychedelic-experience" rel="bookmark">
					<time class="entry-date published" datetime="2022-08-15T10:00:12-04:00">
						August 15, 2022					</time>
					<time class="updated" datetime="2022-08-10T11:57:32-04:00">
						August 10, 2022					</time>
				</a>
			</span>
					<span class="comment-link">
				<span class="prefix">
					with				</span>
				<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/an-orthodox-examination-of-my-foolish-psychedelic-experience#comments">112 Comments</a>			</span> <!-- .comment-link -->
							</div> <!-- .entry-meta .below-title -->
														</header> <!-- .entry-header -->
														<div class="featured-image">
					<a href="https://www.rooshv.com/an-orthodox-examination-of-my-foolish-psychedelic-experience">
						<img width="1060" height="705" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-1060x705.jpg" class="attachment-theblogger_image_size_1 size-theblogger_image_size_1 wp-post-image" alt="" loading="lazy" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-1060x705.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-300x200.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-1024x681.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-768x511.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-1536x1022.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-2048x1363.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-550x366.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-751x500.jpg 751w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-1920x1278.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-1623x1080.jpg 1623w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/magic-mushrooms-psychedelic-600x399.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 1060px) 100vw, 1060px" />					</a>
				</div> <!-- .featured-image -->
													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>In the spring of 2019, approximately two weeks after I started a daily prayer rule upon taking my first steps as a Christian, I took psychedelic mushrooms, something that I would not dare do today. Nonetheless, it happened, and I&#8217;d like to offer commentary on the out-of-body experience I had through the eyes of my growing Orthodox understanding.</p>
<p>Here&#8217;s <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-happened-when-i-took-psychedelic-mushrooms">a recounting of the event that happened</a> while I was under the influence of the mushrooms:</p>
<blockquote><p>I turned to lay on the right side of my body, almost in a fetal position, and closed my eyes once more. The geometric patterns were gone, my vision all black. My breathing became labored once again. My chest felt like it was being wrung out from the center. I tried to be careful with my breaths to make sure I received enough air.</p>
<p>The sound of my breaths was still loud, but now they were becoming spaced further and further apart. Dont be afraid, I said to myself. Then the sound of the air entering my lungs went silent. I was no longer breathing. I could not perceive myself as breathing. I tried to open my eyes, but I couldnt. Then I tried to wave my hands in front of my face, but nothing happened. I was no longer in my body. Then whooshI felt a great movement at amazing speed as if I was transported somewhere else.</p>
<p>I was placed in a great void. My breath was gone, my body was gone. I couldnt hear Albert [my friend] or any sounds of the forest. And yet I was not afraid or worried. There was no concern for what happened to my body or if I would ever possess it again. There was no lamentation that I could not continue experiencing the world as I have for my previous 39 years of existence. In this great void, with no sign of stars or other physical matter, or even the perception of space or time, I felt complete serenity and peace with myself.</p>
<p>Then a large dome with a gray outline came into view. The bottom of the dome was flat. In the center of the flat bottom was a white light. I stared at the light and a warm feeling overcame me. The word home entered my mind. That [could be] the home of my soul, where I came from and where I will go back to, where I will rest for all eternal. I desired to be with the light, to float towards it, but then my eyes opened.</p>
<p>I was back in the forest, curled up on the ground. I took a deep breath and stood up. I wanted to talk to Albert but I had no voice.</p></blockquote>
<p>What happened to my body? What did I see? <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-best-book-for-orthodox-christian-converts">Father Seraphim Rose</a> of blessed memory has offered the most likely answers to these questions in his important book <a href="https://www.amazon.com/Soul-After-Death-Seraphim-Rose/dp/093863514X?&amp;linkCode=ll1&amp;tag=rooshlog-20&amp;linkId=51fc03d2125b24f195935f2d04008449&amp;language=en_US&amp;ref_=as_li_ss_tl">The Soul After Death</a>:</p>
<blockquote><p>[A near-death experience] is not precisely an &#8220;after-death&#8221; experience; it is rather the &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experience which is only the antechamber to other much more extensive experiences, whether of death itself or of what is sometimes called &#8220;astral travelling&#8221; Although the &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; state might be called the &#8220;first moment&#8221; of death&#8212;if death actually follows&#8212;it is a gross mistake to conclude from it anything whatever about the &#8220;after-death&#8221; state, unless it be the bare facts of the survival and consciousness of the soul after death, which hardly anyone who actually believes in the soul&#8217;s immortality denies in any case.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>The beings contacted in this realm are always (or almost always) demons, whether they are invoked by mediumism or other occult practices, or encountered in &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experiences. They are not angels, for these dwell in heaven and only pass through this realm as messengers of God. They are not the souls of the dead, for they dwell in heaven or hell and only pass through this realm immediately after death on their way to judgment for their actions in this life. Even those most adept in &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experiences cannot remain in this realm for long without danger of permanent separation from the body (death), and even in occult literature such adepts are rarely described as meeting each other.</p></blockquote>
<p>From Father Seraphim&#8217;s teachings, my understanding of death and the toll houses as taught by the <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-desert-fathers">Church Fathers</a>, and my own contemplation of the experience, I&#8217;d like to pose three inferences about what happened.</p>
<p>First, I believe that my soul did leave the body for a period of time and enter the aerial realm (the antechamber to heaven or hell). In Church teachings highlighted by Father Seraphim, this is the realm where angels come to take your soul upon bodily death in an attempted ascent to heaven, but if you have failed to please God in your life, your ascent will fail and demons will pull you down to hell. Father Seraphim explains:</p>
<blockquote><p>The realm into which the soul immediately enters when it leaves the body and begins to lose contact with what we know as &#8220;material reality&#8221; (whether after death or in a simple &#8220;out-of-body&#8221; experience) is neither heaven nor hell, but an invisible realm close to earth which is variously called the &#8220;After-death&#8221; or &#8220;Bardo plane&#8221; (Tibetan Book of the Dead), the &#8220;world of spirits&#8221; (Swedenborg and spiritism), the &#8220;astral plane&#8221; (Theosophy and most of occultism), &#8220;Locale II&#8221; (Monroe)&#8212;or, in Orthodox language, the aerial world of the under-heaven where fallen spirits dwell and are active in deceiving men for their damnation. This is not the &#8220;other world&#8221; that awaits man after death, but only the invisible part of this world that man must pass through to reach the truly &#8220;other&#8221; world of heaven or hell. For those who have truly died, and are being conducted by angels out of earthly life, this is the realm where the Particular Judgment begins at the aerial &#8220;toll-houses,&#8221; where the spirits of the air reveal their real nature and their hostility towards mankind; for all others, it is a realm of demonic deception at the hands of these same spirits.</p></blockquote>
<p>If my soul really did leave the body, and this experience is similar to actual physical death, the best analogy I can give to dying is trying to squeeze a marble through a thin straw. Initially, there was the feeling that I was losing gradual awareness and control over my body, including a cessation of sensory feedback, including pain, then a tightness and squeezing in the center of my body as I was being pushed through the &#8220;straw,&#8221; and then a feeling of traveling at rapid speed into another realm, like being blasted off into space. It&#8217;s disconcerting and strange but not painful or frightening. I never lost consciousness or awareness of what was happening, which we would expect because the soul is eternally awake, and the time it took to &#8220;die&#8221; (the progressive shutdown of my body), was short enough that there wasn&#8217;t an opportunity for fear, just confusion as to what was happening. It is possible that real death is a completely different experience, but from my reading of after-death experiences, it seems to be somewhat similar.</p>
<p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-15790 size-large" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-1024x717.jpg" alt="" width="710" height="497" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-1024x717.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-300x210.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-768x538.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-1536x1075.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-2048x1434.jpg 2048w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-1060x742.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-550x385.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-714x500.jpg 714w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-1920x1344.jpg 1920w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-1543x1080.jpg 1543w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/space-tunnel-death-600x420.jpg 600w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /></p>
<p>Second, once outside of the body, my soul enjoyed a feeling of joy and peacefulness since it was unencumbered by sins of the fallen flesh, which was especially true for me since at that time I was riddled with a lifetime of mortal sins that were not yet cleansed through the sacraments of the Church. Father Seraphim shares that once outside of the body, you will experience less of your fallen nature.</p>
<blockquote><p>Our physical bodies in this fallen world are bodies of pain, corruption, and death. When separated from this body, the soul is immediately in a state more &#8220;natural&#8221; to it, closer to the state God intends for it; for the resurrected &#8220;spiritual body&#8221; in which man will dwell in the Kingdom of Heaven has more in common with the soul than with the body we know on earth.</p></blockquote>
<p>Most out-of-body stories of near-death experiences are positive because they describe the soul freely floating in the aerial realm (before any type of judgment takes place). Unless we have lived the lives of saints, our fallen bodies are opposed to the desires of the soul, so coming out of that body feels like taking off tight clothes. Even if you&#8217;re on your way to hell, for the time before the demons come to take you, you will feel free and joyful at the shedding of your flesh. If you&#8217;ve lived a holy life in the body then being out of the body may not offer a stark increase in the joy you perceive, since your body was already subverted to your soul&#8217;s desire to be in communion with God.</p>
<p>Third, I believe the vision I had with a dome containing a white light was either a projection of my preexisting belief of the afterlife or a deception by the demons to trick me into believing pantheistic notions. According to Father Seraphim, afterlife experiences are usually deceptions.</p>
<blockquote><p>most, perhaps indeed all, of [near-death] experiences have little in common with the Christian vision of heaven. These visions are not spiritual, but worldly. They are so quick, so easily attained, so common, so earthly in their imagery, that there can be no serious comparison of them with the true Christian visions of heaven in the past Even the most &#8220;spiritual&#8221; thing about some of them&#8212;the feeling of the &#8220;presence&#8221; of Christ&#8212;persuades one more of the spiritual immaturity of those who experience it than of anything else. Rather than producing the profound awe, fear of God, and repentance which the authentic experience of God&#8217;s presence has evoked in Christians saints (of which St. Paul&#8217;s experience on the road to Damascus may be taken as a model&#8212;Acts 9:3-9), the present-day experiences produce something much more akin to the &#8220;comfort&#8221; and &#8220;peace&#8221; of the modern spiritistic and Pentecostal movements.</p>
<p>[&#8230;]</p>
<p>we must clearly distinguish between genuine, grace-given visions of the other world, and a merely natural experience which, even though it may be outside the normal limits of human experience, is not in the least spiritual and tells us nothing about the actual reality of either the heaven or the hell of authentic Christian teaching.</p></blockquote>
<p>My initial interpretation was that it was a vision from God, because I so strongly craved God at that time, but I no longer believe this interpretation to be absolutely the case because of my then gross impurity and the vague nature of the vision. Visions given by God as described <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-field-of-spiritual-warfare">by Orthodox elders</a> are usually quite descriptive and vivid, not vague and open to multiple interpretations as if it were <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/its-not-easy-to-escape-from-the-occult">a palm reading</a>. For many years before this experience, I had been closely following Zen and Buddhist ideas of the afterlife that detailed the &#8220;collective unconscious&#8221; and going back to the &#8220;source,&#8221; so when I saw the dome, I thought it was the source of all creation, somewhat matching Eastern teachings, but I was so zealous for the real God at the time that I eventually interpreted the vision as being from a personal God. The most neutral possible interpretation is that the dome was something like space junk in the aerial realm.</p>
<p>When someone begins <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/are-you-on-the-path-to-salvation">a life of repentance</a>, they can be given a heavy dose of zeal and often grace. It was while in a state of zealousness that I took the drug and saw the vision, and so I believe that this state blocked me from interpreting it in a way that would steer me away from God. I say this because the psychedelic experience did not veer me off the path to getting baptized into the Orthodox Church <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/why-i-left-the-armenian-church-for-rocor">two years later</a>. I hesitate to say it helped me, but it did allow me to more quickly come to believe in a concrete spiritual reality, in which I had a weak belief at the time. Unfortunately for the vast majority of people, psychedelic experiences more often create mistaken notions of a spiritual reality and pull them away from God into beliefs closely aligned with deism, pantheism, or Buddhism, with the associated universalist belief that &#8220;everyone goes to heaven&#8221; or &#8220;everyone will be in peace after death.&#8221; If this deception is not corrected, a person&#8217;s soul is likely to be damned upon death.</p>
<p>From Father Seraphim:</p>
<blockquote><p>It may be asked: What of the feelings of peace and pleasantness which seem to be almost universal in the out-of-body state. What of the vision of light which so many see? Are these only deceptions also?</p>
<p>In a sense, it may be, these experiences are natural to the soul when separated from the body. Our physical bodies in this fallen world are bodies of pain, corruption, and death. When separated from this body, the soul is immediately in a state more natural to it, closer to the state God intends for it; for the resurrected spiritual body in which man will dwell in the Kingdom of Heaven has more in common with the soul than with the body we know on earth&#8230;. In this sense, the peace and pleasantness of the out-of-body experience may be considered real and not a deception. Deception enters in, however, the instant one begins to interpret these natural feelings as something spiritual&#8212;as though this peace were the true peace of reconciliation with God, and the pleasantness were the true spiritual pleasure of heaven. This is, in fact, how many people interpret their out-of-body and after-death experiences, because of their lack of true spiritual experience and awareness.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<p>I see my psychedelic experience as a form of chemically-induced pseudo-grace. I used a chemical and happened to luck out that I didn&#8217;t have more of a standard experience that would keep me turned away from the Lord God. I attribute this entirely to the fact that I was in a new state of bountiful and genuine zeal at the time and God was closely watching over his idiotic servant. Since then, I&#8217;ve had potent spiritual experiences within the Orthodox Church, without using any type of drug, so it was wholly unnecessary to get blasted off into the aerial realm by using a poison for what amounted to a fireworks show for a man who denied fireworks for much of his life. In fact, I have had spiritual experiences in the body where the joy I felt exceeded the joy felt while out of the body induced by my experience of chemical intoxication, negating any temptation to try a psychedelic drug again.</p>
<figure id="attachment_15791" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-15791" style="width: 710px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-15791 size-large" src="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-1024x768.jpg" alt="Baptism ROCOR Jordanville" width="710" height="533" srcset="https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-1024x768.jpg 1024w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-300x225.jpg 300w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-768x576.jpg 768w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-1536x1152.jpg 1536w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-1060x795.jpg 1060w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-550x413.jpg 550w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-667x500.jpg 667w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-1440x1080.jpg 1440w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902-600x450.jpg 600w, https://www.rooshv.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/06/02_20210509_153902.jpg 1800w" sizes="(max-width: 710px) 100vw, 710px" /><figcaption id="caption-attachment-15791" class="wp-caption-text">Orthodox baptistry</figcaption></figure>
<p>In conclusion, I got lucky, and cannot claim that I saw God or the source of all creation. I did experience something I suspect is close to bodily death, but the vision that followed was likely a demonic attempt to put me back into agnostic or gnostic notions of reality. Thankfully, my hunger for God was so great that I was able to get on the normal path of developing spiritual life as prescribed by Lord Jesus Christ and the Church He created for us, and two years after the experience I was received into that Church. If I hadn&#8217;t typed out <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/what-happened-when-i-took-psychedelic-mushrooms">a record of what happened</a>, I would hardly remember it, signifying how unimportant it was in my path to the Orthodox Church and developing faith in Lord Jesus Christ. Visions under chemical intoxication will not at all compare to what God can give you when He deems you ready.</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/the-law-of-god"><em><strong>The Law Of God</strong></em></a></p>

													<div class="entry-content">
											<p>1. Do Muslims go to heaven? [<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20210411022116/http://www.oocities.org/umaximov/ignat.htm">Link</a>]</p>
<p>2. Dabbling in occultism ruins your mental health [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/129353.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>3. &#8220;We were happy in prison&#8230;&#8221; [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/54147.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>4. &#8220;meekness and humility do not mean spinelessness and should not yield before manifest evil, and that a true Christian should be far from sugar-sweet sentimentality and should not step away in the face of evil&#8230;&#8221; [<a href="https://archbishopaverky.blogspot.com/2011/02/holy-zeal.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>5. The Lives of Saints Cyprian and Justina [<a href="http://orthodoxinfo.com/death/cyprian_justina.aspx">Link</a>]</p>
<p>6. Are Protestants Beyond Hope? [<a href="https://www.patristicfaith.com/orthodox-christianity/orthodox-christian-theology/sola-scriptura-in-the-vanity-of-their-minds/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>7. &#8220;The Lord gives pure prayer to him who, eschewing laziness, prays much and regularly in his own manner, even if it is marred by inattention.&#8221; [<a href="https://orthodoxprayer.org/Articles_files/Brianchaninov-Jesus%20Prayer.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>8. &#8220;Orthodox Christians honor the Theotokos Mary more than all the saints and angels of heaven&#8230;&#8221; [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/88363.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>9. Self-pity corrupts everything we do [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/144055.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>10. &#8220;God gave us the sacrament of marriage as a gift that allows us to attain eternal life through service to and love of another person&#8221; [<a href="https://news.gab.com/2022/01/13/on-christian-femininity/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>11. The Theotokos Prayer Rule [<a href="https://inklesspen.blog/2022/01/20/the-purity-of-the-mother-of-god-and-the-theotokos-prayer-rule/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>12. &#8220;The Apostle Paul counsels us to flee from sexual immorality. Do you hear? Dont even fight with it&#8212;but flee from it!&#8221; [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/142049.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>13. &#8220;Yoga is beneath [the] umbrella of Hinduism, and in many ways is the pole of the umbrella. It acts as a missionary arm for Hinduism and the New Age outside of India.&#8221; [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/80417.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>14. The nature of dreams corresponds to the persons spiritual state [<a href="https://www.pravmir.com/why-shouldn-t-we-believe-our-dreams/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>15. The Pharisee speaks madness in his prayer as he stands before God in the temple [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/144387.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>16. &#8220;They were willing to face even death to uphold their conscience before God&#8221; [<a href="https://inklesspen.blog/2022/02/12/the-way-of-the-warrior/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>17. &#8220;the entire structure of contemporary life in the so-called &#8216;free&#8217; world, where there is no open and bloody persecution of faith, where everyone has the right to believe as he wishes, represents a far greater danger to a Christian&#8217;s soul by drawing the Christian wholly down to earth and making him forget heaven&#8221; [<a href="https://archbishopaverky.blogspot.com/2011/04/life-of-christian-in-our-modern-world.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>18. &#8220;To fantasize about a person is to fail to see the person as a person. Just as in pornography, it is to objectify, to fail to relate, to fail to love&#8221; [<a href="https://ftftl.org/2016/05/imagination-and-fantasy-pornography-of-the-mind/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>19. How God Punishes Nations for Fornication for Many Generations [<a href="https://russian-faith.com/family-values-explaining-orthodoxy/how-god-punishes-nations-fornication-many-generations-n6553">Link</a>]</p>
<p>20. &#8220;The Russian nation in its present capacity, and hopefully, ever more so in the future, is a living reproach for the modern West because we have regained what we once lost while they lost what they once had&#8221; [<a href="https://orthochristian.com/145190.html">Link</a>]</p>
<p>21. The German who went to Rostov and became a Russian Saint [<a href="https://russian-faith.com/video-saints-history/700-years-ago-german-came-rostov-became-russian-saint-n6594">Link</a>]</p>
<p>22. &#8220;True light is rejected because it causes a painful exposure of the true state of humanity and persons&#8221; [<a href="https://deathtotheworld.com/articles/people-today-still-choose-barabbas/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>23. How life continues after death [<a href="http://orthodoxinfo.com/death/unbelievable.aspx">Link</a>]</p>
<p>24. Christianity is a Kingdom, Not a Religion [<a href="https://orthodoxethos.com/post/the-inseparable-union-of-dogma-and-ethos-and-how-christianity-is-a-kingdom-and-not-a-religion">Link</a>]</p>
<p>25. How to read the Bible [<a href="http://orthodoxinfo.com/phronema/ware_howto.aspx">Link</a>]</p>
<p>26. &#8220;[The Orthodox Church] may be the only church which attracts and holds men in numbers equal to women&#8221; [<a href="http://anothercity.org/why-orthodox-men-love-church/">Link</a>]</p>
<p>27. WW1 Ukrainian Priest, Murdered by Austrian Catholics, Made a Saint by Russia [<a href="https://russian-faith.com/saints/ww1-ukrainian-priest-murdered-austrian-catholics-made-saint-russia-n1052">Link</a>]</p>
<p><strong>Read Next:</strong> <a href="https://www.rooshv.com/33-christian-articles-i-recommend"><em><strong>33 Christian Articles I Recommend</strong></em></a></p>
